(2) A 100% tariff must be levied on rayon textiles and rayon-cotton blended textiles and silk textiles. (Japan News Agency dispatch, 7th)

(Tokyo) The Cuban government has increased tariffs on Japanese cloth on the 7th. Cotton textiles are subject to a 25% increase in addition to the highest tax rate, and silk and rayon textiles are subject to a 100% tariff. It is rumored that because cotton textiles are subject to ad valorem duty, a total of 9.84 million square yards were exported from January to March this year, but the future export of Japanese cloth will be quite difficult. This tariff increase is a fatal blow to cloth merchants. Since silk and rayon textiles were originally subject to ad valorem duty, the 100% tariff can be described as a ban on imports. Therefore, the export of Japanese goods will be completely impossible in the future. However, since the export volume has always been minimal, it will not affect the overall situation. (Japan News Agency dispatch, 8th)

Gold and Silver

London Gold Price: Today, it rose 5 pence to 144 shillings and 0.5 pence.

London Silver Bar: The silver market crashed today due to excessive profit-taking by speculators and a lack of support. The measures include strictly implementing general denunciations to eradicate the roots of poisonous plants; banning sales by cracking down on raw opium shops and enforcing strict management; banning smoking by setting deadlines for registration and gradually reducing the number of smokers; and banning transportation by the Anti-Smoking Inspection Office, which is responsible for strictly following Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's six-year anti-drug policy to completely ban it. This time, the order to ban opium is extremely serious. Anyone who violates the opium ban will be shot without exception. It is hoped that the public will be awakened to automatically quit and not ignore it, lest they fall into the clutches of the law. Subsequently, Committee Member Zhang Gangfeng made a detailed report on the gradual implementation of anti-smoking measures and plans to imitate Jiangsu's anti-smoking model by establishing designated smoking areas to show restrictions. As for party, government, military, and public officials, as well as school staff and students, smoking is absolutely prohibited, and they must obtain joint and several liability pledges. If anyone is found smoking, they will be shot without exception and without leniency. (7th Central News Agency)

Disputes over Coal Mine Boundaries in Liujiang 85

Japanese Military Police Demolish Light Railway, Construction Department Orders Linyu County Magistrate to Negotiate

Tianjin Correspondence: At around 9:00 AM on the 4th of this month, more than 30 Japanese policemen from Qinhuangdao and Yuguan, led by Sato, the chief of the Japanese Police Station in Dongluocheng, Shanhaiguan, along with a squad of Japanese military police, forcibly sealed off the pier and warehouses of the Liujiang Coal Mine in Qinhuangdao and demolished the railway connecting Qinhuangdao to the Liujiang mining area. At that time, a passenger train on the line was about to start, but it was forcibly stopped by the Japanese military police, and all the passengers on the train were driven off, cutting off transportation. Because it was difficult to transport coal, the Liujiang Coal Mine stopped work on the afternoon of the 4th, and the manager telegraphed the Construction Department, requesting a speedy negotiation to avoid long-term losses. Yuan Tai, the magistrate of Linyu County, met with Sato, the chief of the Shanhaiguan Japanese Police Station, and Ishida Hisatomo, the Japanese manager of the Taiki Coal Mining Company, who was involved in the incident, and discussed the matter. The Japanese side also did not want the negotiation to escalate and planned to resolve it locally. Magistrate Yuan came to Tianjin on the night of the 4th to ask for instructions from the provincial government's Construction Department and decided to return to Linyu on the night of the 6th to invite all parties involved to discuss the matter.

The cause of this incident was investigated as follows: The Liujiang Coal Mine is a commercial joint-stock company, and its major shareholder is Liu Hongsheng, the general manager of the Shanghai China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. The mine's smokeless coal is one of the leading mineral products in North China and is sold throughout the country. The business is very good. A light railway of more than 40 li was built from Qinhuangdao to the mining area. In addition to transporting coal, it also handles passenger and freight transportation. It has been in operation for more than 20 years. The mining area covers more than 4,000 mu. Adjacent to it is the Taiki Coal Mining Company, whose original license holder was Sun Jiwu. It was approved by the Ministry in the third year of the Republic of China. Later, Sun formed a Sino-Japanese joint venture with the Japanese, with Sun as the Chinese chairman and the Japanese, Ishida Hisatomo, as the Japanese chairman. The mining area also occupies an area of 4,000 mu. However, since obtaining the license, although mining has been carried out, it has been repeatedly interrupted. In March of this year, Ishida claimed that since Jiwu had died, he planned to start operations himself. However, because the coal seam was slightly inferior to Liujiang, fearing that the output would not be strong, Ishida, based on the unclear replacement map from the sixth year of the Republic of China, strongly argued that the Black Stone Nest mining area, which is adjacent to the two mines and covers an area of about 1,000 mu, belonged to Taiki. The two sides argued privately several times, but without results. Later, Ishida filed a complaint with the Tianjin Consulate, which was forwarded to the Shanhaiguan Police Station and the Linyu County Magistrate for negotiation (because the two mining areas are south of the Great Wall and are both under the jurisdiction of Linyu County). The Linyu County Magistrate forwarded the details to the Construction Department, which checked the mining law and the Ministry's records and found that Liujiang Coal Mine's mining of the Black Stone Nest mine did not infringe on any facts. Just as the Linyu County Magistrate Yuan Tai was ordered to handle the matter, the Japanese military police, led by Ishida, demolished the railway and sealed off the warehouse as a threat. Yuan Tai returned to Linyu to negotiate under the order of the provincial government's Construction Department. As for the outcome, it depends on the attitude of the Japanese side. (6th)

Conditions of Relief Undertakings in Guangdong Province 86

Essential Work in the Administration Plan, Provincial Government Allocates Funds to Assist Counties in Handling

Guangzhou Correspondence: Guangdong Province, in accordance with Article 11 of the Founding Program, has clearly defined relief undertakings as essential work in the administration in the three-year administration plan, and the Civil Affairs Department is actively supervising its implementation. In addition to allocating funds for disaster relief in the event of temporary disasters and ordering various counties to sort out warehouse storage and store grain to prepare for famine, strictly prohibiting adulteration to maintain people's food supply, special attention is paid to supervising various counties to handle old-age homes, infant care centers, public hospitals, and pauper asylums, etc., in accordance with the current three-year plan. Because various counties have difficulty raising funds, they have also been ordered to handle matters flexibly, combining old-age homes, orphanages, orphanages, pauper asylums, and hospitals into relief homes to handle various relief matters, or to run public hospitals separately. However, most counties are poor and have difficulty raising funds. Few counties have established or prepared relief homes and public hospitals in the 23rd year of the Republic of China. Therefore, in January of this year, it was approved that counties that can raise funds locally to establish or prepare various institutions will be given a subsidy of 200 yuan each by the province. Counties that have received this subsidy include Longmen, Chixi, Heshan, Chaoyang, Chenghai, Xingning, Lechang, Qujiang, Lianshan, Wuchuan, Suixi, and Wenchang for the funding of the establishment of relief homes, and Huaxian, Conghua, Deqing, Longchuan, Lufeng, Dapu, Xingning, Wuhua, Haifeng, Chaoyang, Chenghai, and Wenchang for the funding of the establishment of public hospitals. However, most counties are unable to raise funds to establish various institutions, so they submitted a request to the provincial government, requesting a large amount of funding to be allocated in stages as funding for the establishment of relief homes and public hospitals. It is estimated that Lianping, Fogang, Jiaoling, Lezeng, Ruyuan, and Kaijian will each receive 4,000 yuan, and Haifeng, Raoping, Beixian, Dapu, Yangshan, Heping, Wengyuan, Longmen, Xinfeng, Xuwen, Lingshui, Pingsu, Lianshan, Qiongdong, Ganen, Changjiang, and Nanao, 17 counties, will each receive 3,000 yuan, Huiyang, Qujiang, Hepu, Lingshan, Xinyi, Xingning, Lufeng, Yingde, Lianjiang, Boluo, Qinxian, Heyuan, Zengcheng, Puning, Nanxiong, Wuhua, Yunfu, Suixi, Huilai, Deqing, Longchuan, Enping, Yunan, Lianxian, Zijin, Yaxian, Dingan, Sihui, Wanning, Xinxing, Chengmai, Fengshun, Huaxian, Shixing, Lingao, Baoan, Wuchuan, Lechang, Gaoming, and Renhua, Chixi, 41 counties, will each receive 2,000 yuan, Guangning, Huaxian, Dianbai, Conghua, Fengchuan, 5 counties, will each receive 1,000 yuan, Meilu Administration Bureau 1,000 yuan, and Lianyang Huayi Bureau medical expenses 1,000 yuan, for a total allocation of 164,000 yuan.

Currently, the counties that have achieved more success in handling relief undertakings are: Panyu Old-Age Home, which houses more than 60 poor elderly men and women; the Skills Training Center, which houses more than 150 apprentices; Nanhai Foshan Relief Home, which houses more than 80 orphans; Jiujiang Relief Home, which houses more than 50 poor men and women; Heshan Relief Home, which houses more than 110 poor men and women; Zengcheng Infant Care Center, which houses about 20 female infants; Yunfu Old-Age Relief Home, which houses more than 30 poor men and women; Infant Care Center, which houses about 20 female infants; Huilai Infant Care Center, which houses more than 10 female infants; Luoding Infant Hall, which houses 16 female infants; Guangning Relief Home, which houses 37 poor men and women; Gaoyao Relief Home, which houses 49 poor men and women; Heyuan Relief Home, which houses 16 poor men and women; Zengyang Old-Age Home and Pauper Asylum, which house more than 60 poor men and women; Infant Care Center, which houses 72 infants; Dongguan Relief Home, which houses 112 orphans; Deqing Infant Care Center, which houses 26 infants; Shunde Relief Home, which houses 135 poor people and 30 homeless elderly people. In addition, Daliang Infant Care Center and Chencun Infant Care Center, the number of housed is not known; Chaoan Pauper Asylum, which houses 291 poor men and women; Infant Hall, which houses 46 female infants; Conghua Relief Home, the number of housed is not known; Qingyuan Infant Hall, which houses 22 female infants; Chenghai Infant Care Center, the number of housed is not known; Old-Age Home, which houses more than 10 poor men and women; Gaoming Old-Age Home, which houses 18 poor elderly men and women; Haikang Old-Age Home and Disability Center, which house more than 50 poor elderly people and disabled poor people; Qi Infant Center houses seven female infants; Maoming Relief Home and Universal Relief Home house over 100 poor men and women; the Infant Care Center houses eight female infants; Shantou Pauper Labor Arts Institute, which houses 477 homeless poor people, 90 orphans, 108 poor elderly people, and 113 disabled poor people.

As for the counties that have been planning to establish public hospitals or public hospitals, there are 49 counties and cities, including Panyu, Nanhai, Dongguan, Shunde, Zhongshan, Xinhui, Taishan, Baoan, Zengcheng, Qingyuan, Sihui, Chixi, Gaoming, Guangning, Heshan, Kaijian, Fengshun, Lufeng, Chaoyang, Jieyang, Chenghai, Huilai, Nanxiong, Lechang, Shixing, Maoming, Xinyi, Lianjiang, Haikang, Yangjiang, Yangchun, Qiongshan, Dingan, Lingshui, Fangcheng, Lingshan, Luoding, Kaiping, Yunfu, Yunan, Huiyang, Boluo, Chaoan, Xingning, Qujiang, Wengyuan, Yingde, Dianbai, and Shantou. Other unformed relief homes and public hospitals are still being urged to prepare for establishment.

The Civil Affairs Department has now promulgated the Relief Home Organization Rules, stipulating that each county and municipal government must establish a relief home to handle old-age homes, orphanages, disability homes, infant care centers, medical clinics, and loan centers, etc. The management of equipment in each institution and the procedures for entering and leaving the institution are clearly stipulated and must be supervised by the county government. The loan center is specifically for those who do not have bad habits and are willing to start a small business. If they have the above-mentioned aspirations and have a guarantor or equivalent guarantor, they will be given a loan of five to twenty yuan, without interest. After that, they will repay it in installments on schedule. If they fail to repay it on time, the guarantor will repay it on their behalf. If there are special circumstances, it can be handled according to the circumstances. If this relief home can be promoted and expanded, not only will the lonely and helpless each find their place, but the unemployed poor will also be reduced. As for the rules of the relief home, the most important thing is the provision of funds. The funds of the home are supplemented by local income and donations. However, the fund should be organized by local legal groups to elect a number of people to form a fund management committee to manage separately. All immovable property must be approved by the competent authority before it can be sold. In this way, there is not only a source of funds, but also strict supervision and management, so that there will be no corruption or self-enrichment.

76 Notorious Bandits in Jiaodong Executed 87

Xu Rongzhang and 4 Other Bandits Beheaded Inside the Provincial Government, the Remaining 69 Escorted to the Execution Ground for Justice

Jinan Correspondence: In order to pacify Jiaodong, Han Fuju, chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government, specially appointed Liu Yaoting, captain of the Third Route Special Detective Team, as the guerrilla commander of Jiaodong last month to go to more than ten counties in eastern Shandong, including Gaomi, Jiaozhou, Jimo, Pingdu, Changyi, Zhucheng, and Rizhao, to carry out the work of eliminating bandits, combining suppression and appeasement to achieve lasting peace. After Liu received the order, he set up an office to work. The famous Jiaodong bandit leaders Xu Rongzhang, Shi Linfu, Guo Bingzhong, Guo Pijian, and Shan Yizhi surrendered one after another. Xu and others had been bandit leaders for seven or eight to ten years, leading hundreds to two or three thousand bandits. They claimed to have turned over a new leaf, willing to serve the local area, and take full responsibility for Jiaodong's security and bandit suppression. Currently, there are 74 bandits who have all been concentrated in Gaomi. After Liu Yaoting contacted them in many ways and completed the formalities, he followed Han Fuju's order and transferred all 74 bandits to Jinan to await inspection and training. It was originally planned to incorporate them into a detective team to serve the local area and be responsible for eliminating scattered bandits in eastern Shandong. Unexpectedly, although Xu and other bandits had surrendered, they still secretly left a group of followers in the Jiaodong area, secretly kidnapping and extorting ransoms, selling tickets, and other illegal activities. A few days ago, they even kidnapped more than a dozen students in Jimo. Liu Yaoting discovered the matter and reported it to Han Fuju and Shi Jingzhou, director of the Military Law Department of the headquarters. At the same time, the detectives of the detective team also hated Xu and other bandits and were unwilling to associate with them. After receiving the report, Han Fuju believed that Xu and other bandits were so lawless, which was extremely heinous, and ordered that Xu and other bandits be executed to show a warning. After receiving the order, Liu Yaoting brought Xu and others to the Military Law Department inside the provincial government at 6:00 PM on the 6th under the pretext of training. With an order, Liu Yaoting directed the detectives to behead Xu Rongzhang, Shi Linfu, Guo Bingzhong, Guo Pijian, and Shan Yizhi in the courtyard. At the same time, he tied up the remaining 69 bandits, including Sun Jingshan, and escorted them to an empty space outside Nanweimen, verified their identities, and completely shot them. The execution was completed by 8:00 PM. All those who were tied up and taken to the execution ground were handled by the members of the detective team, who were swift and agile. The names of the bandits who were shot are recorded below: Bandit leaders Xu Rongzhang, Shan Yizhi, Shi Linfu, Guo Bingzhong, Guo Pijian, notorious bandits Zhang Zifu, Guo Zixiu, Dong Yuntian, Yu Dengyuan, Guo Cunhe, Pan Shaojiu, Li Baichuan, Chu Jilu, Tang Qishan, Yu Zhanhao, Dong Yunmei, Yu Shengzhi, Zhang Qingdao, Zhang Derui, Guo Jincheng, Li Jiuchun, Sun Mingshan, Zhang Minggong, Sun Baolong, Dong Shuqi, Sun Ruiting, Liu Youlu, Kuang Guangchun, Wan Xuchang, Wu Jinzhi, Dou Xuekong, Wu Yongcai, Gao Yueshou, Yin Dexin, Xue Fuzhen, Xu Shuqing, Wu Xisheng, Guo Xuli, Lu Xicai, Sun Jingshan, Dai Jusheng, Sun Weiting, Leng Xitang, Dai Zengshan, Chen Fushan, Zhang Fuxun, Liu Futian, Gao Huan, Wang Jinyu, Wang Zifa, Liu Bulin, Wang Mingshan, Zhang Junyan, Zhang Yunting, Wu Xiaofeng, Zhang Yuanxiu, Gao Zhenming, Zhang Zhongjing, Zhang Ziyu, Gao Zengtang, Wang Fengting, Liu Xidong, Zhang Shouxu, Shi Yudong, Shi Yulu, Cui Naiqi, Hua Kun, Leng Fubin, Gao Cunben, Wan Demi, Liu Shouxian, Zheng Zhiguang, Li Taichen, and Wan Renchen. (6th)

Notorious Bandit of Southern Shandong, Zhang Black Face, Brought to Justice (Continued) 88

The Special Detective of Shandong captured Zhang while he was hiding in Anhui Province, and after interrogation by Han Fuju, he was immediately executed.

Zhang terrorized the border regions of Shandong and Jiangsu, leading over ten thousand men, causing havoc for nearly twenty years. Now that he has been captured, he is attracting great attention. Recently, our reporter paid a special visit to the headquarters of the Special Detective Brigade to interview the bandit Zhang and inquire about everything. The Detective Brigade brought Zhang to the room to meet the reporter. Zhang is not very fat, only of medium build, with a refined appearance, dark complexion, and a short, bristly beard. It is fitting that he is known as Black Face. He wore a light gray short coat, stained with oil, with blue cloth trousers, gray socks, and blue cloth shoes. He was in good spirits and looked amiable, but his eyes flashed with ferocity. He spoke with a Jiaxiang (Shandong Province) accent, with slight Jiangsu and Anhui tones. He talked and laughed freely, as if unaware that he was a prisoner. The reporter invited him to sit down and asked about his past as a bandit and his current thoughts. Zhang spoke freely about the past, saying that he had been a bandit for nearly twenty years, money came like water, and he squandered it like dirt. He had been a highwayman for half his life and had no savings. His eighty-year-old father had no means of support, which he deeply lamented. Zhang also stated that he was currently forty-six years old, from Dongzhuang Village, sixty-five li north of Yixian County (now part of Tengzhou), Shandong Province. His ancestors were farmers and originally good, honest people. He still has an elderly father, Zhang Yunrang, who is eighty-two years old, living in Peikou. He has one wife and three daughters, living in XInji, Lingbi County, Anhui Province. His original name was Zhang Jiadong, also known as Zhang Jiansheng. After becoming a bandit, he was called Zhang Black Face because of his dark complexion. The nickname became well-known in the underworld, and his real name was forgotten. In the seventh year of the Republic (1918), he lived in Dongzhuang Village, Yixian County. He had an older brother, Zhang Jiayi, who served as a soldier under Zhang Xun in the Dingwu Army. When he returned home to visit his family, it happened that his cousin, Zhang Kaikin, was murdered. The county authorities accused his brother of the murder, arrested him, and imprisoned him, where he died of cold and starvation. Feeling deeply aggrieved and impoverished, he joined Wang Yutang, a bandit leader from Gaozhuang, Yixian County. Soon after, the Lincheng train robbery occurred, and Sun Meiyao was appointed to recruit new troops. At that time, Zhang already led seven or eight hundred bandits. Knowing that recruitment was unreliable, he did not participate. Soon after, Sun Meiyao was executed, and the remnants of his band scattered. Zhang took the opportunity to recruit his old subordinates. At this time, Liu Heiqi also rose as a bandit. Zhang and Liu were on par with each other, and there was talk of the "Two Blacks of Southern Shandong." Not long after, Wang Yutang died of illness, and Zhang's forces grew even larger, numbering seven or eight thousand, even ten thousand men, terrorizing the border regions of Shandong, Jiangsu, and Anhui. Zhang's fifth brother, Zhang Jiade, nicknamed Manbazi, was the most ferocious bandit under Zhang's command, having led troops to capture cities such as Ju County and Yishui County. Later, Liu Guitang repeatedly offered recruitment, but Zhang never participated. During the Northern Expedition of the Revolutionary Army, Zhang's troops remained in the mountains. In the twenty-first year (1932), Chairman Han (Fuju) recruited Liu Guitang, Guo Mafeng, Yin Shigui, and Yin Shishan, gathering them at Dawenkou, living in Gaotang. Xia Ziming and others went to the mountains to offer recruitment to Zhang's troops, which at that time numbered about seven or eight thousand men. They gathered at Dongguozhuang, more than twenty li east of Teng County. First, seven or eight hundred men boarded trains to advance north, but when they arrived at Xiache Station, they heard that Liu Guitang had fled from Gaotang, so they also got off the train midway and fled into the Mengshan and Culaishan mountains, scattering their weapons. Zhang also stated that the most notorious bandits under his command were all his adopted sons, including Li Doujin, Li Douyin, Mao Xuetian, Sun Yewen, Li Yingxiang, Song Guixin, Xu Yude, and thirty others, who were the most famous. Li Doujin and Li Douyin were brothers, leading over a thousand bandits. Mao Xuetian led over a thousand bandits. Sun Yewen led several hundred bandits. Li Yingxiang led over a hundred bandits. Song Guixin led seven or eight hundred bandits. Xu Yude led over two thousand bandits. The rest each led several hundred to a thousand men. Most have died, scattered, or fled. The Li brothers are already dead, leaving only Mao Xuetian, who still leads two or three hundred men, in the border areas of Jiangsu. However, in southern Shandong, Teng County, Yixian County, Linyi, Yicheng, Fei County, Ju County, and Rizhao, those who act as bandits are all under Zhang Shaoqian and no others. Zhang finally said that after leaving Shandong, he lived in Xinmaqiao, north of Zaozhuang. Unexpectedly, his luck had waned, and he was captured and brought here. Although he had been a bandit for nearly twenty years and had seen a lot of money, he had given it all to friends and had no savings. His eighty-two-year-old father had no means of support. If Chairman Han would show kindness and give him a chance to reform, he could gather two or three hundred of his old subordinates to serve the local area, ensuring peace and tranquility in the Teng, Yi, Lin, Fei, Ju, and Ri areas, eliminating banditry, and so on.

At 8:00 PM on the 5th, Provincial Chairman Han Fuju personally interrogated Zhang Black Face, Sun Yewen, Liu Yuzhen, and others in his office. Liu Yaoting, the captain of the Special Detective Brigade, transported the three bandits from the brigade headquarters to the Provincial Government by car to await interrogation. Han first interrogated Zhang Black Face. Upon seeing Han, Zhang immediately asked, "Is this the Governor?" Han slightly nodded his head. Zhang then said, "I really feel sorry for having disappointed the Governor with the previous recruitment." Han said, "That is in the past, it is nothing." Han slowly asked how many years he had been a leader. Zhang confessed, "I have been in charge for about seventeen or eighteen years." Han asked, "Have you accumulated any savings from being a bandit for so many years?" Zhang confessed, "Since I became a bandit, I have received no less than several hundred thousand dollars, but I have always been fond of making friends and spent it all. I have no savings now." Han then asked, "Are there still people in your family?" Zhang confessed, "I still have an elderly father, a wife, and three daughters." At this point, Han ordered them to be taken down to rest. He then interrogated Sun Yewen. Han asked how many years he had been a bandit. Sun confessed that he had been a bandit since the thirteenth year of the Republic (1924), which is already more than ten years. Finally, he asked Liu Yuzhen how many years he had been a bandit. Liu confessed that he had been a leader since the seventh year of the Republic (1918), which is already seventeen or eighteen years. During the Northern Expedition of the Central Army, he was once recruited by the Central Army and served as a battalion commander, regimental commander, clan leader, and other positions, and had led troops to capture counties such as Yishui. Han ordered them all to be taken down. Han, considering that all the bandits had committed heinous crimes, sentenced them all to death, specifying that they would be executed by firing squad at 7:00 AM on the 6th. However, Han also believed that although Zhang Black Face and others were bandits, they were generous by nature and worthy of being considered heroes. However, due to the law of the land, they could not be spared. He specially ordered that thick coffins be prepared for their bodies, and that they be buried in deep pits. He also ordered that Zhang be informed before the execution so that he would know. He further ordered that Shi Jingzhou, the director of the Military Law Department, and Liu Yaoting, the commander of the Special Detective Brigade, be responsible for handling the matter. At 7:00 AM on the 6th, before the bandits were executed by firing squad, it was feared that since Zhang and others had been rampant for many years and had many followers, unexpected incidents might occur. Therefore, soldiers from the pistol brigade and enforcers from the Military Law Department, a total of forty men, were dispatched to guard everything. Military judges Qiao Langting, Zhang Qiao, Yang Jinqing, and Deputy Commander Feng Xiuan of the Special Task Force were appointed as execution supervisors. At 7:30 AM on the 6th, the execution supervisors and troops arrived at the Public Security Bureau and brought out the three bandits, Zhang Black Face, Sun Yewen, and Liu Yuzhen. After a brief interrogation, the bandits were tied up and put into cars, riding in three cars in total. The first car carried soldiers from the pistol brigade, the second car carried the bandits, and the third car carried the execution supervisors. They left the Public Security Bureau and headed to the Houjia Dayuan execution ground on Weiba Road. Upon arriving at Houjia Dayuan, troops had already been stationed around the area to provide security. The three bandits were then ordered to kneel facing south. Zhang Black Face was on the east side, Sun Yewen was on the west side, and Liu Yuzhen was in the center. Their identities were verified at the same time, and they were executed by firing squad simultaneously. The bandits all faced their execution generously, without saying a word. Zhang and Liu were each shot twice, and Sun was shot once. The executions were completed by 8:30 AM. The government provided coffins for their bodies and buried them, and also telegraphed their families to come and claim the bodies. (The End)

18,000 Stone of Rice Allocated to Forty-Eight Disaster-Stricken Counties, Including Lihuang

Songjiang: Road Construction Cuts Off Water Supply, Farmers Appeal 90

Since automobiles have been travelling on the Songwei County Road, transportation has been very convenient. Recently, the expansion of the Songjiang to Sijing County Road began with contracting out the construction of culverts and road surfaces and has already begun work. It is expected that it will be open to traffic in mid-June, and transportation in Songyi will become even more convenient in the future. However, the farmland in Shijiutu and Baiwo Township, including the 18th Tu, 10th Gang, and 11th Tu, is divided into two parts by the road. The originally planned number of culverts is insufficient, and it is feared that the fields traversed by the road will not have enough water for irrigation and will become barren. It is difficult to irrigate them by detouring to scoop water, and it is unbearable to watch them become barren. Therefore, the township chief Chen Liuzhang and landowners Wang Zhilin, Yu Zhongchi, Yang Tianjue, and others have successively petitioned the district office to forward their request to the county government, which is in charge of the road project, for prompt relief. The acting district chief Lu Dai believes that the farmland in that area is within the scope of the road construction and that the tenants have suffered losses. The addition of water pipes to connect the farmland irrigation is indeed an essential plan. He has already submitted the case to the county government to be reviewed and to promptly provide relief to alleviate the farmers' hardships.

Suzhou: A Fire Burns Down, Kills Elementary School Student 91

A fire broke out at No. 11 Chuanxin Street, Hulong Street, at 2:30 PM on the 7th. The fire was very fierce and burned down a total of sixty-two thatched houses, belonging to twenty-five households. An eight-year-old elementary school student from Jiangbei named Gao Dalong was unable to escape and perished in the fire. The disaster victims were all from Jiangbei, and their cries shook the wilderness with a scene of utmost misery. Fortunately, the broker Yin Guang showed great compassion and distributed money to the disaster victims, totaling three yuan per person. Yesterday (the 8th) afternoon, the District Procuratorate sent Inspector Chang to examine the body of Gao Dalong, ordering that a coffin be prepared and the body be collected.

Transfer of Japanese Consul-General in Suzhou 92

The Japanese Consul-General in Suzhou, Kawaminami Seiichi, has been ordered to be transferred to Yunnan as consul. His successor will be Kawanishi Toyomi, who is scheduled to arrive in Suzhou on the 20th of this month and take office on the 21st. Consul-General Kawaminami is currently handling the handover procedures. County Magistrate Wu Qiyun has scheduled a banquet at the county government on the 15th to bid farewell to Consul-General Kawaminami.

Wuxi: Records of Water and Land Robberies 93

Dian Dequan from Teng County, Shandong Province, makes a living by selling bamboo poles by boat. Three days ago, he sold the bamboo poles and obtained more than four hundred yuan. He bought flour and white rice and loaded them onto the boat at Gongyun Bridge to sell bamboo poles in Yixing. When he arrived under Wuqiao Bridge, it was late, so he moored on the riverbank in front of Yongcheng Timber Shop, preparing to sail early in the morning. Unexpectedly, at about 1:00 AM, four or five deckhand robbers pushed the boat into a small canal in Shuanghejian and robbed it. They stole 347 silver dollars, 42 current silver dollars, three bags of flour, five dou of white rice, and five clothing bags, with a loss of more than 500 yuan. Also, the family of Hua Songkui, a resident of Di Yi Township, near Tangkou Town in the Eighth District, was robbed by seven or eight thieves at 1:00 AM the night before. The thieves scaled the walls and entered the house, tied up the owner, and robbed at will, losing more than 100 yuan. Also, yesterday, in Taiping Township in the Third District, five refugee boats carrying more than two hundred refugees landed at Dabaolong Bridge and robbed the home of the neighborhood chief Fei, stealing all the clothes and ornaments, as well as all the chickens and ducks in the village, with incalculable losses.

Yufeng Yarn Factory in Yuxi Experiences a Five-Hour Work Stoppage 94

The Yufeng Yarn Factory in Lihua Village recently hired a type of female instructor. They are responsible for instructing new and old female workers in spinning skills, and have dismissed thirteen male workers who are habitually lazy. On the other hand, the factory strictly instructed the supervisors of both the coarse and fine yarn departments to earnestly urge the workers to work, in order to improve the products. The factory also reduced the wages of the workers as appropriate, but the workers were quite dissatisfied with this, which led to a strike. Yesterday morning (7th) at 5:00 a.m., when the day and night shifts of the factory were changing, the workers in the coarse yarn department suddenly stopped the machines and stopped working first. Before long, the workers in the fine yarn department also rose up in response. The yarn factory employees all fled. The workers also poured out of the factory, gathered in the trade union for a meeting, and then returned to the factory, demanding that the factory restore the reduced wages to their previous levels. At that time, the order was chaotic. The factory's workshop, general affairs office, security department, test and examination department, and dormitories were destroyed. At that time, the county party department, public security bureau, and security team received the news one after another, and sent personnel to the scene to suppress and persuade the workers to resume work first. The workers returned to the trade union and put forward four conditions: (1) to reinstate the dismissed workers; (2) to dismiss Gao Hengzhi and Yan Futing, supervisors of the workshop, and Huang Peichang and Lu Zaishen, staff members of the security department and the work accounting office; (3) to restore the previous wage rates; and (4) to dismiss the newly hired female instructor. They demanded that the factory immediately respond. Zhou Jimei, the manager of the factory, agreed to reply after convening a shareholders' meeting on the 19th of this month. The county party department members repeatedly advised the workers to resume work first. The four requirements would be answered by the 20th. The workers were satisfied and resumed work at 10:00 a.m. In total, the strike lasted for five hours.

Changzhou: Provincial and Departmental Committees Inspect and Accept River Works 95

The Seventh Construction Section of the Dredging Zhenwu Canal Work Relief Office has been working diligently since the start of construction, and the entire project is nearing completion. Among them, the section near Qiya Weir is a prosperous area for commercial transport. The people of that town, seeing that the river works have been completed, requested that the dam be opened early to facilitate transport. Upon receiving the report, the Provincial Government specially appointed Inspector Zhao Lie and Construction Department Committee Member Cheng Qitang to arrive in Changzhou at noon on the 7th. Section Chief Shi Ziquan accompanied them to Qizhen to complete the acceptance. At the same time, the dams at Sanshan Port and Mei Port were also accepted and opened on the 8th. From now on, transport will be smooth and commercial transport will be convenient. The river works from Qizhen to Luoshe section can also be completed within a few days.

The Jiangsu Provincial Branch of the China Islamic Association held its second provincial committee meeting at 9:00 AM on May 5th at the Jiangdu County Islamic Branch in the Majian Lane Mosque in Yangzhou. Submit a request to the provincial party and government organs for subsidies; 2. Before funding is determined, the committee members will temporarily advance the funds; (2) The association's budget is distributed according to the following table: 47% for project expenses, 53% for administrative expenses; (3) How should the association respond to the insulting text published in the Wuxi Xinmin Daily? (Decision): 1. Submit a request to the party and government organs for severe punishment; 2. Appoint committee members Liu Binru and Hua Ruzhou to draft a refutation; (4) Urge all counties to establish preparatory committees within a time limit (Decision): Officially establish the preparatory committees before May 31st; (5) Appoint personnel to conduct district inspections of association affairs (Decision): Appoint standing committee member Yang Gongya and committee member Dai Baichuan to draft inspection outlines, which will be submitted to the next standing committee for discussion; (6) All committee members of the association should abide by the decisions of the congress, set an example, first follow the teachings, pay Zakat (charity), and establish religious and social undertakings (Decision): Send a letter to all committee members to earnestly comply; (7) How should we handle the Jiangdu County branch member Jin Xun's request to fight for people's land by telegram? The Tuntian (military farmland) dispute in Jiangdu, where the landlord and tenant farmers fiercely argued over rent during County Magistrate Cao's tenure, has not been thoroughly resolved. Zhenjiang: Relief for Farmers Whose Land Was Requisitioned 99

The Su Province Guidance Huai River into the Sea project is progressing smoothly. In order to facilitate the project and ensure smooth water flow, the Provincial Government previously adopted the method of cutting off bends and straightening the waterway, requisitioning about 10,000 mu of private land. Farmers who depend on the land for their livelihoods are inevitably affected. In order to seek redress, the authorities specially designated over 20,000 mu of official wasteland near Qitao in Lianshui as a reclamation area to compensate the farmers for the requisitioned land. A technical officer, Zhang Binzhen, was dispatched by the Reclamation Design Committee to investigate. He is expected to return to the province soon. Once the investigation of the land surface, soil quality, and the number of relocated farmers in the reclamation area is completed, the entire plan will be drawn up and implemented as soon as possible.

The Zhenjiang Party and Government Joint Electrical Price Reduction Evaluation Committee held a meeting on the afternoon of the 6th. As for the establishment of a public meter station, the Construction Bureau is actively preparing for it.

Nantong: Summons of Party Affair Meetings for Nine Counties 101

Zhang Gongren, the Jiangsu Province Fourth District Party Affair Supervisor, will hold a meeting of party heads from the subordinate counties of Nantong, Rugao, Hai'an, Qidong, Chongming, Jingjiang, Taixing, Jiangyin, and Changshu on the 10th, where they will discuss advancing social projects and setting up party member training courses.

Jiangbei's Wheat Harvest is Reduced 102

The wheat harvest in the Jiangbei region, including Tongtai and surrounding areas, was affected due to the warm winter and the unusually cold spring with snowfall. The wheat crop is now being harvested, but yields are reduced by an estimated 40%. The spring bean harvest is expected to be only 60% to 70% of normal.

Jiangyin: Discovery of a Young Girl's Corpse at Tangtou Bridge 103

On the southern end of Tangtou Bridge in the Sixth District, not far from the Jinghe River on the border of Wuxi, the corpse of an unidentified young girl was discovered. The girl was approximately fifteen or sixteen years old and appeared to be from a poor family. The township chief Xue Pinquan reported the incident to the Qingyang Public Security Station and the county. On the 6th, the trial officer Gu Cheng and the coroner Cao were sent to the village to examine the body. The girl's right arm and right leg both had bruises and wounds from wooden objects, indicating that she had been beaten before being thrown into the river and drowned. Her underwear had the words "Jiangsu Provincial Water Police Fourth District" printed on it. The Jia chief had the corpse coffined and buried, as there were no family members, it was provisionally buried in the charity tomb. According to villagers, the girl was a child bride from the Shi family in Shichuang. Her maternal family was from Yucheng, Danyang, and she took her own life due to abuse by her in-laws. Trial officer Zhou Cheng instructed the township chief to investigate the family and report to the district for transfer to the county for handling.

Xishan: Taozhuang Silk Merchants Robbed Twice 104

Zhang Jusan, a silk merchant in Taozhuang Town, is well-off. Last spring, his business was robbed by lake bandits, with losses of over a thousand yuan. Unexpectedly, on the 1st of this month, several more lake bandits arrived and robbed his business again, stealing all the clothes and utensils in the house, with significant losses. The local police and militia have been notified to strictly pursue the bandits.

Three Fires in One Day 105

The weather has been dry recently, and fires have been heard of in various villages. Yesterday, three fires occurred in one day: (1) At the home of township chief Zhou Yixing in Tianren Village, a careless cook caused a fire that burned down five houses, resulting in significant losses. (2) The kiln house of Wu Fufu, a kiln owner in Hongjiatan, was also destroyed by fire, resulting in a loss of over one hundred gold coins. Zou Shen Jinsheng was seriously injured while fighting the fire. (3) A fire also broke out at the home of Zou Yutian in Fugi Village, burning down five flat houses in front of the house.

Jiaxing: Major Fire in Nanhui Township 106

At around 11:00 PM on the 6th, a fire was set by thieves at the home of Sheng Guisheng in Yihang, two li from Nanhui Town in northern Jiaxing. The fire spread to over sixty houses and more than ten households. The Nanhui fire brigade arrived and worked hard to put out the fire, which was finally extinguished on the 7th at dawn. The estimated loss is over 30,000 gold coins.

Huaiyin: Prisoners Escape from the Gao Branch Court Detention Center 107

Zhang Tongyi, age 36, a bandit from Lianshui, and Xie Debiao, age 28, from Yiyun, were detained in the detention center of the First Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. They had been sentenced to fourteen years in prison by the Zhongyuan County Court, and they had appealed. At 12:00 AM on the 4th, they escaped by climbing over the wall. The guards on duty at the time were Dai Jinbiao and Zu Deren. It was not until 3:00 AM on the 5th, when the guards changed shifts and checked the number of prisoners, that the escape was discovered. The warden was notified and sent people to search everywhere, but no trace was found. Yesterday (the 5th), the detention center sent photos and records of the two prisoners to the Huaiyin Public Security Bureau for investigation.

Xiaoshan: Robbery in the Fourth District 108

Yang Yuansheng, a farmer from Yangcun Village in the Fourth District of Xiaoshan, is diligent and frugal and has a small amount of property. His kinsman, Yang Jianbang, also lived in the same house. Unexpectedly, at midnight on the 4th, six local bandits, speaking in a local accent and carrying local rifles, broke into the house by digging a hole in the wall. Two bandits stood guard, while the others went upstairs and ransacked the boxes and chests, taking whatever they wanted. The family members were awakened from their sleep and were too stunned to speak out. The bandits left at will. As a result, Yang Yuansheng's family had three trunks stolen, as well as copper and tin items. Yang Jianbang's family also had daily necessities stolen. The total estimated value of the stolen goods is over 300 yuan.

Unstable Weather Leads to Prevalence of Epidemics 109

Recently, the weather in Xiaoshan has been unstable, with alternating cold and heat, leading to the prevalence of diseases such as diphtheria and typhoid fever. The strong can resist the effects, but the weak are infected and their lives are at risk. In the Sanjun area outside the South Gate, over twenty people have died. General Chinese and Western doctors are extremely busy.

Hangzhou: Business Failure Leads to Suicide by Opium Ingestion 110

A certain Jin, a 26-year-old native of Hangzhou and advertising director for a Hangzhou newspaper, made over ten thousand yuan two years ago through managing advertisements. After his term expired last year, he resigned and went to Shanghai to continue in the advertising business. Unexpectedly, he lost over ten thousand yuan. Returning to Hangzhou after this failure, he developed thoughts of ending his life. On the 7th, he ingested a large amount of opium at home in a suicide attempt. After being discovered, he was sent to the Municipal Hospital for treatment, but due to the severity of the poisoning, he died at 9:30 PM. His family prepared a coffin and arranged for burial.

Consultation on the Implementation of the American Economic Mission 111

The Zhejiang Provincial Tourist Bureau and the Hangzhou Municipal Government, acting on the orders of the provincial government, prepared to host the American Economic Survey Mission. As the mission is scheduled to arrive in Hangzhou on June 3rd, a meeting of various agencies and organizations was convened at the Construction Bureau yesterday (the 8th) at 10:00 AM. Over ten representatives from Zhejiang University, the Municipal Government, the Bankers' Association, the Silk Industry Association, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce attended. The following resolutions were made: (1) Promotional materials will be jointly printed by various agencies and organizations, and banquets will be hosted separately by each; (2) Expenses for hospitality, transportation, accommodation, and mountains will be shared equally by various agencies and organizations, while banquet costs will be borne individually; (3) The reception program will be revised.

Ningbo: Hengfeng Dyeing and Weaving Factory Suddenly Runs Aground 112

The Hengfeng Dyeing and Weaving Factory, located outside the South Gate of Ningbo, is a large-scale operation with a history of prosperous business. Recently, the number of male and female workers has increased to 700. In addition to spinning and weaving, two new departments for raising nap and printing and dyeing were added last year. However, due to the expansion of the business scope, the silver reserves became strained, leading to a temporary cash flow problem and causing it to run aground. The amount owed to various firms is estimated at over 300,000 yuan, bringing the total debt, including firm debts, to 780,000 yuan. The inventory, including dyes, is valued at approximately 590,000 yuan. All fixed assets, including land, buildings, and machinery, are valued at 540,000 yuan at purchase price. In reality, there is no deficit. The factory is scheduled to hold an emergency shareholders' meeting today to discuss ways to maintain operations.

Haimen: Rampant Banditry in the Third District 113

The third district of this county, bordering Kunshan, Lianyun, Nantong, and the eastern townships, was ravaged by communist bandits in 1930, suffering significant losses. To this day, the local vitality has not recovered. Now, at this time between harvests, bandits are taking advantage of the situation, and there have been over ten robbery cases in the district in the past month. The people fear retaliation from the bandits and dare not report to the authorities, leading to rampant banditry. Several days ago, a group of bandits was secretly plotting an uprising in the wheat fields near Lion Town. However, the district police force learned of this, went to search and arrest them, and they scattered and fled.

Local News

Today is the May 9th National Humiliation Memorial Day: The Entire City Flies Flags at Half-Mast and Suspends Entertainment in Mourning 114

Today is the May 9th National Humiliation Memorial Day. In addition to issuing a public notice, the Municipal Party Headquarters has published an announcement in the newspaper, convening representatives from all sectors of the city to hold a memorial meeting at 9:00 AM, and has appointed committee member Zhao Xion as the chairman of the assembly. The entire city will fly flags at half-mast in mourning and suspend entertainment for the day. The Chinese and Concession police authorities will implement special martial law. Details are as follows:

Notice of Commemoration

The Municipal Party Headquarters issued a notice in the newspaper to convene a memorial meeting. The original text reads: "Notice: May 9th is the National Humiliation Memorial Day. This headquarters will convene representatives from all sectors at 9:00 AM on this day in the assembly hall of this Party Headquarters to hold a memorial meeting. This is a special notice, requesting that all agencies, organizations, schools, and Party headquarters at all levels in this city each send two representatives with letters to participate, and uniformly suspend entertainment and fly flags at half-mast in mourning. This is a special notice."

Suspension of Entertainment

Today is the National Humiliation Memorial Day. In addition to the memorial meeting convened by the Municipal Party Headquarters, all entertainment in the city will be suspended. All cinemas and amusement parks will be closed. It is reported that the theaters and amusement parks in Nanshi, including Penglai, Gonghe, Fuan, Xiaoshijie, Zhabei Shijie, and Weiyang, will be completely closed today in mourning.

Half-Mast and Alert

The Municipal Party Headquarters has also notified all sectors of the city to fly flags at half-mast in mourning. At the same time, in order to prevent disturbances by reactionaries, a special request has been sent to the Municipal Public Security Bureau to implement martial law. It is reported that the Municipal Public Security Bureau has ordered all branch bureaus and police stations to increase patrols and has ordered inspectors, detectives, and male and female inspectors to set out separately for close patrols. The intersection of Chinese and Concession areas is under especially tight security. The public and French Concession police authorities have also separately ordered all constabularies to strengthen their defenses to prevent disturbances.

Ministry of Finance Decides to Reduce Transit and Other Taxes on June 1st 115

Measures for reducing and exempting export taxes have been drafted, and standards for domestic goods have been established.

Xinxin News Agency reports that the issue of abolishing transit taxes and reducing and exempting export taxes has been submitted by the Ministry of Finance to the National Tariff Commission and the Customs Administration for the respective authorities to draft implementation measures. These measures have now been drafted and will be implemented starting June 1st after the new tariff regulations are submitted to the Legislative Yuan for review and approval. Details are as follows:

Abolition Measures

After the principle of abolishing transit taxes was approved by the Central Political Council, the Ministry of Finance issued it to the competent authorities to draft implementation measures. These measures have now been drafted and approved for implementation starting June 1st. It is reported that after the implementation of this new system, inland customs will also be abolished in conjunction. In the future, all imported goods will be taxed by coastal customs, but one or two Jianghai Customs will be selectively retained in important locations along the Yangtze River to handle upstream and downstream inspections and anti-smuggling matters to prevent tax evasion. The Ministry of Finance is currently conducting a thorough study on this matter.

Tariff Regulations Drafted

The issue of reducing and exempting export taxes is even more the only crucial plan for developing foreign trade. After Minister of Finance Kong submitted it to the Central Political Council for approval, the Ministry of Finance stipulated reduction and exemption standards and instructed the National Tariff Commission to refer to the original tariff regulations for detailed research and draft new tariff regulations. This has now been drafted and submitted to the Ministry of Finance for review and will be forwarded to the Legislative Yuan for review and approval. The National Government will then issue a formal announcement and implement it starting June 1st.

Reduction and Exemption Standards

According to sources, in addition to drafting new export tariff regulations, the Tariff Commission has also established several standards for domestic goods. If the raw materials are domestic, the manufacturing is done by Chinese, the capital is Chinese, or the capital is Chinese, the manufacturing is done by Chinese, and a small amount of foreign raw materials are used, one can state the difficulties encountered and provide detailed reasons, whether due to the decline in international trade, the opening of overseas markets, dumping by other national goods, or temporary excessive costs. They can all be submitted to the Ministry of Finance for review, and after sending personnel for on-site investigation and confirmation, they will be approved separately according to the export tax reduction and exemption standards.

This Year's International Labor Conference: Our Side Prepares Important Proposals; Various Groups Host Farewell Banquets for Delegates Leaving the Country 124

Central News Agency reports that the delegates attending this year's International Labor Conference are scheduled to depart on the 10th, and various parties are currently hosting farewells. A Central News Agency reporter learned that our side's proposals for this conference are as follows:

Restricting Dumping to Save Decline

The most important proposal prepared by our side this time is regarding the policy of dumping. In recent times, various countries in the world have been increasing the production of goods as much as possible, reducing the cost of goods on one hand, and dumping them abroad on the other. This policy is detrimental to the domestic labor force, as it reduces wages and increases working hours. Furthermore, the result of their dumping has further caused our country to fall into a state of industrial and commercial recession and increased unemployment. This proposal will request the conference to formulate restrictions on dumping policies. In addition, the issue of factory inspections in the concessions will also be submitted to the International Labor Organization authorities for early implementation.

Selling Chinese Laborers is Inhumane

Youth unemployment has become a serious problem in our country. This time, some statistics on this issue have been collected and prepared to be submitted to the conference to request the deliberation of relief measures. Many Chinese laborers have been sold to Nanyang and other places as coolies. Treating people as livestock is truly inhumane and will also be raised. The proposal on equal treatment for colored laborers, which was proposed by our country's delegate Ma Chaojun at the previous conference, will be further elaborated. The above proposals may have some difficulties in implementation, but for the sake of the interests of our country's labor force, it is said that the delegates will still work hard to coordinate.

Foreign Merchants Offering Small Life Insurance Policies: Government to Ban Them 127

The Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau of the Ministry of Communications, in order to facilitate the general working class, has planned to offer simple life insurance, which has been approved by the Legislative Yuan and is scheduled to be implemented on July 1st. However, foreign merchants have recently imitated this, which is in conflict with our country's laws. According to sources in the Postal Savings Bureau yesterday, it was reported the other day that the American-registered American Foreign Life Insurance Company recently founded small life insurance by Yang Shupai, which is quite similar to the simple life insurance founded by the Postal Savings Bureau. Simple life insurance is life insurance. In European and American countries, it is called industrial life insurance because its wages are paid weekly and its premiums are also paid weekly. The purpose of the simple life insurance offered by the Postal Savings Bureau this time is to seek the interests of the people, not to make profits. It has been approved by the Legislative Yuan and is scheduled to be implemented on July 1st. Last month, the Legislative Yuan passed the Simple Life Insurance Law, the first article of which stipulates that simple life insurance is a state-run enterprise, and other insurance companies may not operate it. That is, no company may operate small insurance policies below 500 yuan, which is very clear. The small life insurance offered by the foreign merchant American Foreign Company is quite in conflict with the law passed by the Legislative Yuan. In order to maintain state-run enterprises and the solemnity of the law, the government will ban it.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Telegrahs the Ministry of Finance Requesting Increased Import Taxes on Foreign Goods 128

Should Ensure That the Sales Price of Foreign Goods That Can Be Replaced by Domestic Goods Does Not Decrease to Below the Sales Price of Domestic Goods

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, based on the proposal of Executive Committee member Hu Xiguo, telegraphed the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing yesterday to increase import taxes on foreign goods that can be replaced by domestic goods: "Ministry of Finance: In recent times, the trend of the world economy has shifted from tariff wars to trade management. Under this import quota, it is equivalent to the elimination of imports, and on the other hand, the policy of reducing currency values and abolishing the gold standard is used to create an unprecedentedly cheap record for foreign exports in order to occupy other people's markets. Unfortunately, our country is caught in the middle of these two major policies. Over the past decades, the gradually created modern industry will be completely submerged by this frenzy. Anyone who is familiar with domestic and foreign business conditions has this feeling. If the current tariff policy is not changed and all foreign goods that can be replaced by domestic goods are subject to increased import taxes so that their sales price does not decrease to below the sales price of domestic goods, then the existing factories in the country will have no chance of revival. This matter is even more fundamental and essential than providing loans for relief. Only hope that your ministry will resolutely preside over and approve the requested handling. It would be the great fortune of the industrial community. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, respectfully. Yang."

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Letter to the Court Explaining: Delivery Receipts Do Not Need Stamps 131

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, to clarify that delivery receipts are not merchandise vouchers issued by shops, and therefore, according to the provisional regulations, do not require stamp duty, specifically sent letters to the Shanghai Local Court and the Second Branch of the Higher Court for explanation. The two letters are as follows:

Letter to the Local Court

In direct reply: We received your letter of the 7th of this month, forwarding the ministry order to temporarily suspend stamp duty on delivery receipts for reference. Upon investigation, Article 2, Category 1 of the current Provisional Stamp Tax Regulations only stipulates stamp duty for cash receipts, and does not stipulate stamp duty for merchandise receipts. Therefore, such documents have never been affixed with stamps, and there has never been any penalty for violating the regulations. Last year, the Legislative Yuan deliberated and the government promulgated the Stamp Tax Law on December 8, which included both cash and merchandise receipts, stipulating that both should be stamped. In fact, the law has not yet reached its effective date and has not yet come into force. However, general enforcement personnel misunderstood the intention of the law and frequently sent such cases for penalties. In order to avoid misunderstandings by public officials, our Chamber presented a request to the Ministry of Finance and received the above-mentioned instruction. The so-called temporary suspension of stamp duty is because once the Stamp Tax Law is implemented, merchandise receipts will naturally require stamps. Because the time is very short, the word "temporary" is used to distinguish it. Following the previous letter, we enclose a copy of the Ministry's instruction and briefly describe the background of this matter. We request your court to take note.

Letter to the First Branch Court

In direct reply: On the 7th of this month, we received a letter from the Municipal Color Printing Industry Association stating that on the 4th of this month, member Heji Printing Company reported that in February, the Public Works Bureau, following an order from the Special District Court, came to inspect account books and vouchers to see if any stamp duty had been omitted. As a result, 104 delivery receipts from Zhu Hongji and Heji were taken away, and 8 unused ones were recorded. Subsequently, the court imposed a fine of 1,100 yuan on the 15th of the month. Upon investigation, these delivery receipts were in triplicate form. The first copy was the delivery note, given to the customer, and was stamped. The second copy was the receipt, which the customer stamped and returned as proof of receipt of the goods. The third copy was the stub. Upon investigation, the Provisional Stamp Tax Regulations do not specify any stamp duty for delivery receipts, and the Ministry of Finance has a clear order to temporarily suspend stamp duty, so there is no need to affix stamps. Therefore, an appeal was filed according to law. Subsequently, on April 8, an appeal ruling was issued, stating that the second copy of the receipt is a merchandise voucher issued by a shop as described in Category 1, Item 8 of the Provisional Stamp Tax Regulations, and is also a voucher that should be stamped. Except for the 8 unused receipts that were exempted from penalty, the remaining 104 receipts were still subject to a fine of 1,040 yuan. According to the regulations, a merchandise voucher issued by a shop is issued when a customer purchases goods but does not take them immediately. The shop then issues a merchandise storage voucher so that the customer can pick up the goods later with the voucher. This is completely different from the nature of a delivery receipt, which is a merchandise receipt. Moreover, the phrase "issued by a shop" in the case of a merchandise voucher issued by a shop clearly means that the voucher should be held by the recipient as proof. As for the delivery receipt, it is still collected by the shipping shop as proof that the customer has received the goods. The two cannot be compared at all, which is very obvious. The court is not familiar with business practices and misinterprets these provisions, which is a mistake. Although the appeal ruling is wrong, the merchant's suffering has no way to be addressed. The current state of commerce is such that even with year-round operations, it is difficult to obtain even a small profit. Now, because the court misquotes the provisions, the merchant is suffering and has no way to appeal. Is this the intent of the legislation? As a last resort, we specially send this letter to you, urging you to forward it to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to seek relief, and send separate letters to the court and the tax bureau, to understand the difficulties of businesses and to allow for correction. Based on this, it is found that the receipt used by Zhu Hongji, which is Heji, is in triplicate form. The first copy is the delivery note, given to the customer, and has already been stamped. The second copy is the receipt, which the customer stamps and returns. Since it is a merchandise receipt, according to the current Stamp Tax Regulations, there is no explicit provision for it, so it can be temporarily exempted from stamp duty, and it is absolutely different from the merchandise voucher issued by a shop as described in Category 1, Item 8 of the Provisional Stamp Tax Regulations. The statement in the letter from Heji Printing Company, which is Zhu Hongji, is very clear. Accordingly, we report the situation truthfully, urging your association to seek relief, and send a letter to the court and the tax bureau, allowing for correction, which is fair. Upon investigation, a merchandise voucher issued by a shop is received by the customer for future pick-up from the shop, such as deposit slips, reservation slips issued by bookstores, dyeing slips issued by dyeing shops, and receipts issued to customers by photo studios and clock repair shops. All of these belong to this category. As for the delivery receipt, it is a receipt that the customer should issue to the shop after receiving the goods. The main party is the customer, not the shop, and what matters is the customer's stamp. Otherwise, it is just a blank receipt pre-printed by the shop for the customer, which has no evidentiary effect on the voucher. Based on this, it is absolutely not considered a merchandise voucher issued by the shop. Therefore, there has always been an order from the Ministry of Finance stating that it is a merchandise receipt, which is not specified in the Provisional Stamp Tax Regulations and does not require stamp duty. However, although this case has already gone through appeal procedures and there is no way to obtain further relief, the issue concerns the standard for stamp duty penalties. For the sake of future remedies, we accordingly send this letter to your court, asking you to pay attention to it and hoping that your court can investigate such cases with the Ministry of Finance and the Tax Bureau at any time, which would greatly benefit businesses. To the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court.

The instruction speech of Committee member Yang Hu of the association is recorded below. Comrades, representatives, regarding the conference of responsible persons of the lower-level party departments convened by our association recently, I was unable to attend the opening ceremony because I had just returned to Shanghai from Beijing and was limited by time. I am very sorry, but I am very happy to be able to meet with all of you comrades at this closing ceremony. We know that the significance of convening this conference by our association is, on the one hand, to make a general report and a general review of our past work, to serve as an observation and a lesson. Furthermore, comrades, the difficulties or questions you feel in various places can all be brought here for resolution. On the other hand, we want to use this meeting to determine our future work policies and to give us some warnings and excitement, and to advance the seamen's party work on a bright path. We now hope that through the efforts of all of you comrades after this meeting, we can achieve this goal. But now I still have two points of view that I hope all of you comrades will do. First, we must tighten the organization of the party. The Special Party Department of the Chinese Seamen has only been established for more than two years. The history is short, and the work is complicated. In the future, I hope that everyone will tighten up the organization of the lower-level party departments of the seamen, making them as solid as iron, so that they can become a vital force in the revival of the nation. Second, we must step up the training of seamen. In the past, seamen were limited by economics and could not get a good education from the country. In the future, all of you comrades must work hard to train them, so that they can become a healthy citizen in private and a warrior who defends the nation in public. Comrades, the international situation is urgent, and the Third World War is about to break out in an instant. We are responsible for the seamen’s wartime transportation and reconnaissance responsibilities. The responsibility is very heavy. We must be able to mobilize the entire population in wartime. We must work hard during peacetime. I hope that all of you will return to your districts and work hard, so that you will not fail the party and the country, and serve the country. Today I can’t talk much because of something. Finally, I wish you all hard work, finished.

Pudong Public Office Letter States Opinions on Dismantling Dongjiadu Wooden Wharf 135

The Pudong Public Office raised funds to build a public cement wharf at Dongjiadu, and two public wooden wharves on either side. Since the Public Utilities Bureau borrowed it to set up the Shipping Affairs Office and the Shipping Donation Office, and the long-distance bus Liuliqiao ferry occupied the public wooden wharf on the south side, only the public wooden wharf on the north side was used for the berthing of ships from Pudong West, passenger ships, and cargo ships. Now the Public Utilities Bureau mistakenly intends to dismantle this public wooden wharf. The Pudong Public Office has sent a letter to the Public Utilities Bureau, asking it to consider the convenience of merchants and people coming and going to load and unload goods, and to avoid dismantling it for the convenience of transportation. The letter draft is recorded below. Dear Sirs, according to the report of Xi Amao and others from Dongjiadu, the wharf management office inspector ordered the demolition of the reed mat shed on the north public wooden wharf of the Dongjiadu cement public wharf on the 5th of this month. The reed mat shed has been demolished on the 7th. They also ordered the demolition of the public wooden wharf within three days. Upon investigation, this public wooden wharf was built by the Pudong Public Office through fundraising. Since the cement public wharf was used by the Public Utilities Bureau to set up the Shipping Affairs Office, the Finance Bureau to set up the Shipping Donation Office, and the South Public Wooden Wharf was used by the South Long-Distance Bus Liuliqiao ferry for berthing, this North Public Wooden Wharf is the only one relied upon by ships from Zhoupu Zhangjiang Zha Xian Nantai and other townships, as well as passenger ships, civilian ships, and cargo ships from various towns in Pudong West for loading and unloading. It is impossible to do without a wharf for even a moment. Inspector Tang did not understand that the reed mat shed was to shelter merchants and people from the wind and rain, and suddenly ordered its demolition, which was already very painful. If he wants to demolish the wharf again, there must be a temporary wharf before people can come and go to load and unload. Moreover, this public wooden wharf was built by the Public Office, and Amao is not in a position to demolish it on its behalf. For this reason, we are reporting to the Public Office. According to this, if the demolition is carried out, a temporary wharf should be built first to avoid obstructing transportation, which is indeed the case. If a temporary wharf cannot be built first, and it hinders dredging of the Pu River, we ask that you comply with the will of the people and consider the demolition so that ships can still come and go to load and unload. For the sake of inter-agency harmony, we still request a reply. To the Wharf and Warehouse Management Office of the Shanghai Public Utilities Bureau, Pudong Public Office, May 8.

Yongxing Money Exchange Case: Court Orders Withdrawal of Criminal Lawsuit 144

Yongxing Money Exchange at No. 11 Xingren Lane, Lane 120, Ningbo Road, declared bankruptcy on October 20 due to unsustainable real estate business. Lawyers were appointed for liquidation. Xu Baolin, manager of the Tianjin Yujin Bank Shanghai Branch at No. 266 Yongheng Building, Ningbo Road, deposited more than 16,700 yuan into the exchange on April 18 and 19. However, the exchange declared bankruptcy on the 20th. He believed that the exchange knew it could not sustain itself and still accepted deposits, which constituted fraudulent misappropriation. Therefore, he hired lawyer Zhang Deqin to file a criminal lawsuit against the exchange's manager Chen Jingtao, assistant manager Wang Hanqing, shareholders Chen Meibai, Chen Zhongchi, Guo Ruoyu, Chen Dizhou, and six others at the First Special District Court. Yesterday afternoon, First Special Court Judge Xiang Yinghua summoned them in the Second Criminal Court. In addition to Chen Jingtao, who appeared in person, none of the other defendants appeared. Lawyer Xu Zuyan was appointed to appear in court as their representative. Xu Baolin first stated, "I paid in more than 16,700 yuan in drafts on the 18th and 19th, and Yongxing closed down on the 20th. The defendants knew that it would close down on the 20th, so they should not have accepted my money on the 19th. Therefore, their actions did constitute fraud." Chen Jingtao stated in his defense that he had a good relationship with the plaintiff, and there were frequent dealings between them, with mutual deposits and debts. This closure was simply because the exchange invested in many real estate businesses. When it needed funds, it could not pledge them, resulting in unsustainable turnover, and therefore, it was forced to close down. As for the plaintiff's charges, it was entirely a civil dispute, which could be pursued in the civil court. After Judge Xiang's investigation, he ordered the plaintiff to withdraw the criminal lawsuit and file a civil lawsuit instead. Xu Baolin agreed and declared that he would withdraw the complaint. Judge Xiang ruled that the court would not accept the case.

Manufacturing and Selling Syringes and Needles Regulations 145

The regulations for manufacturing and selling syringes and needles by Western medicine merchants and medical equipment merchants in this city have been submitted to the Municipal Government for promulgation. The transcript is as follows: (1) Any Western medicine merchant or medical equipment merchant within the city who intends to manufacture, import, or sell syringes and needles shall, in addition to complying with the Provisional Regulations for the Administration of Syringes and Needles amended by the Executive Yuan, also comply with these regulations; (2) Western medicine merchants and medical equipment merchants who intend to manufacture, import, or sell syringes and needles shall first apply for registration with the Municipal Health Bureau in accordance with the Regulations for the Administration of Medicine Merchants by the Ministry of Interior, the Provisional Regulations for the Administration of Syringes and Needles amended by the Executive Yuan, and the Registration Regulations for Medicine Merchants and Medical Equipment Merchants of this city. They may only operate after being approved for registration and issued a license. Those concurrently engaged in manufacturing syringes and needles shall submit a prior request to the Municipal Health Bureau for record-keeping and may only commence manufacturing after approval; (3) Western medicine merchants or medical equipment merchants concurrently engaged in manufacturing syringes and needles shall submit a list of each batch of products to the Municipal Health Bureau for approval before they can be sold; (4) When selling the aforementioned products, Western medicine merchants and medical equipment merchants concurrently engaged in manufacturing shall comply with the following procedures: 1. When purchased by a formal physician, hospital, or medical institution, a certificate with a signature and seal is required; 2. When ordered by a formal Western medicine merchant or medical equipment merchant, in addition to providing a formal purchase certificate with signature and seal, an application form for ordering medical equipment approved by the Municipal Health Bureau is required before the sale can be made; 3. The aforementioned purchase certificate shall be reported periodically by the seller to the Municipal Health Bureau for review; (5) Formal Western medicine merchants and medical equipment merchants who intend to order syringes and needles from other places for the purpose of import and sale shall first obtain an application form from the Municipal Health Bureau, fill it out according to the format, and submit it to the bureau for approval. After the approved quantity for ordering has been reviewed and approved, the approved application form will be returned to the original applicant before an order can be placed with the manufacturer; (6) When syringes and needles ordered from abroad arrive at customs, the bill of lading and invoice shall be submitted to the bureau for inspection along with the previously approved application form for ordering medical equipment. After verification that the quantity matches the originally approved quantity, the application form will be cancelled, and a Certificate for Approved Medical Equipment will be issued, which can be used to collect the goods at customs; (7) The procedures for formal Western medicine merchants and medical equipment merchants to sell syringes and needles shall be carried out in accordance with the provisions of Articles 4 and 5 of these regulations. For syringes and needles consigned to other locations, a formal certificate filled out by the purchaser shall be submitted to the bureau for review in advance. Only after a Certificate for Approved Consignment of Medical Equipment has been approved and issued can the consignment be made; (8) If there are any omissions in these regulations, they may be amended with approval at any time; (9) These regulations shall take effect from the date of approval and promulgation.

Military Officer Accused by Concubine, Requests Withdrawal After Trial Begins 146

Deng Jianhao, a former high-ranking military officer, when stationed in Hubei in previous years, often took advantage of his spare time from military affairs to dress casually and visit Wuhan. He fulfilled his wish of offering a jade pendant, taking Liu Meiying as a concubine. At that time, Liu was only fifteen years old, beautiful both inside and out. Deng favored her greatly, so wherever his banner pointed, whether south or north, he would take this "Madam" with him. It wasn't until March of the year before last that they moved to Shanghai together, building a golden house to hide her beauty.
