However, he dared not appear in court to confront the accuser. Recently, he vacated the rented residence and secretly took his beloved concubine to room 429 of the Nanjing Hotel on Shanxi Road, hoping to evade legal sanctions. But from then on, he could not help but vent his anger on Liu, starting with daily quarrels, followed by him leaving alone, abandoning her and treating her like a stranger. First Batch of Crated Tea Arrives in Shanghai 150

Last year, there were over 240,000 crates; this year, an increase is expected.

The Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway has historically transported large quantities of crated tea produced in the provinces of Zhejiang, Anhui, and Jiangxi annually. This crated tea is specifically supplied for export, with Russia being the largest destination. Due to seasonal factors, this year's new crated tea has been released earlier than usual. It is now known that the first batch of crated tea is being transported by the Huitong Transportation Company and is being reported and loaded in batches from the Zhakou Station to Shanghai. Over the past two days, over 1,780 crates have arrived at the Shanghai South Station, unloaded from the train. These crates are handled by over 20 tea merchants from the mainland, including Yongxingxiang, Cheng Dafeng, Tongxingxiang, Hengtaihe, and Yonghuachang, and are delivered to Shanghai tea merchants such as Yongxinglong, Gong Shengyong, Shenyuan, Zhongxin Chang, Yuanfeng, and Runqianji. After arriving at the station, the crates are transported by the Huayun Company to the Yuanji Foreign Warehouse on the Suzhou Creek in northern Shanghai for storage and then successively declared for export and sold overseas. Last year, the total number of crated tea transported by this railway was over 240,000 crates. It is expected that this year's transportation will increase compared to previous years.

Wuxi Red Pill Case: Principal Offender Arrested in Shanghai 151

Photo Identifications Confirmed, Wuxi Sends Personnel to Arrest

In September of last year, the Wuxi County Public Security Bureau detected and dismantled a "Red Pill" (amphetamine) manufacturing facility in Shirangjun Alley in the city, seizing red pills and machinery, and arresting five suspects. Under interrogation, they confessed that the principal offender of the facility was Wang Guiqing from Anhui, who had fled. The five suspects were handed over to the military court for punishment according to the law. At the same time, a photograph of Wang Guiqing was obtained, and an arrest warrant was issued. However, after escaping from Wuxi, Wang Guiqing secretly fled to Shanghai, fearing discovery by the authorities. He used the alias Zhang Kexiang, initially staying in hotels, moving frequently, and acting mysteriously. Later, he rented a room in Shanchang Lane on Carter Road, living in seclusion to avoid detection. Until recently, about two weeks ago, Wang, believing that the situation had eased after more than half a year, moved to a pavilion room on the upper floor of No. 36 Hongxiang Lane on Xinzha Road, living alone in seclusion. However, this was discovered by inspectors Ge Xinde and Feng Yimao of the Wuxi Public Security Bureau, who reported it to the bureau chief. Two official letters were prepared, one addressed to the Xinzha Police Station and one to the First Special District Court, requesting assistance in the arrest, along with the warrant and Wang's wanted photograph. At around 9:00 AM the day before yesterday, they traveled to Shanghai by car and submitted the letters to the Xinzha Police Station, stating everything and requesting assistance. The police chief sent detectives Ruan Yao and Xing Lai to arrest Wang Guiqing at the address, seizing a letter and taking him to the police station. Yesterday morning, Qian Xunjiu, the police station's lawyer, presented the case, stating that when the defendant was arrested, he denied being Wang Guiqing and claimed to be Zhang Kexiang. Later, personnel from the Wuxi Public Security Bureau identified the defendant as Wang Guiqing and presented the wanted photograph for verification. A torn letter from an accomplice in Wuxi was also found in the wastepaper basket, asking the defendant for four sums of money. He was taken to the police station, where he admitted that his real name was Wang Guiqing and that Zhang Kexiang was his alias. He also confessed that he was in charge of the Wuxi Red Pill facility and fled to Shanghai after the incident. The Shanghai Municipal Council agreed to the extradition. Subsequently, inspectors Ge Xinde and Feng Yimao of the Wuxi Public Security Bureau submitted official documents, presented evidence, and requested permission to transfer the suspect. The defendant's testimony was evasive. After reviewing the evidence, Judge Yang Zhao ordered that Wang Guiqing be handed over to the Wuxi Public Security Bureau personnel for return to Wuxi for interrogation and trial.

Yu Huogen's Son-Killing Case Prosecuted 152

Yu Guanhong (also known as Yu Jilin), son of Yu Huogen, a villager at No. 2 Xinzhaizhi, Yujiatang, west of Hongqiao, Shanghai, was addicted to morphine injections and, more recently, to smoking red pills. He was lazy and refused to work, and committed many evils, causing his family to hate him intensely and refuse to share food with him. As a result, he wore tattered clothes and went out to beg during the day, returning home at night to sleep. His father, Yu Huogen, due to his son's unfilial behavior and persistent refusal to change despite repeated admonitions, and his recent descent into begging, which had severely eroded his face, conceived the idea of killing his son. On the night of April 12th of this year, he colluded with his daughter-in-law, Yu Chen (Yu Guanhong's wife), to strangle Huogen to death with a rope. After the incident, the local police station detained Yu Chen, the murderer of her husband, and sent her to the district court for interrogation and detention. Prosecutor Lei Binzhang arrived on the scene to conduct an examination and confirmed that he had been strangled to death, ordering a coffin to be prepared for burial. In fact, the perpetrator was Yu Huogen, who should have been arrested and detained. However, it was discovered that he was suffering from severe dropsy, so he was not detained. At the time, it was ordered that he be handed over to the local security chief for supervision pending further instructions. Details of this were recorded in a previous report. It is now learned that the case has been investigated and confirmed by Prosecutor Lei Binzhang, who has filed charges of homicide with the criminal court, requesting a public trial. Yesterday, the presiding judge ordered the security chief of the 28th Bao, 1st Tu, Chen Wentang, to inform Yu Huogen to surrender to the court at the appointed time to await trial.

Shen Jifeng's Suicide Case Investigated 155

Deceased Wife Found Innocent, Released

The circumstances surrounding the death of Shen Jifeng, a rickshaw puller from Yancheng, who lived in a flat adjacent to the Xizhongxing Cotton Mill on Zhongxing Road, Zhabei, who allegedly stabbed himself in the chest with a sharp blade due to suspicions of his wife's infidelity, have been reported in the newspapers. It is now learned that due to time constraints on the day of the incident, Wang Shaoting, the security chief of the Jin Er Tu area, did not report the death for investigation. Therefore, it was not until yesterday morning that a report was submitted to the Shanghai District Court requesting an investigation. At around 5:00 PM, Prosecutor Zhang Zi was dispatched to the scene. He found that the deceased, Shen Jifeng, had indeed died from injuries sustained during his lifetime. A burial permit was issued, instructing the security chief to arrange for the coffin and burial. It is also learned that Shen Qi, the deceased's wife, was sent to the Xinzha Branch Bureau by the Taiyangmiao Police Station. Bureau officer Ouyang Liu took her statement, in which she stated, "My husband drinks several times a day. This morning, he was drunk and said that I had come home too late yesterday (Tuesday) from my mother's house. He scolded me and hit me and wouldn't let me cry. He took a knife to stab me, but I rolled on the ground, and he couldn't stab me. So, he stabbed himself. Many people saw it but couldn't stop him. We don't usually argue much, only once last year," and so on. After reviewing the statement, the interrogating officer reported it to the Inspectorate of the General Bureau for further review after the court's investigation. The investigation was completed yesterday, so the officer ordered that Shen Qi be released and that the details be reported to the General Bureau for record.

Xinzha Branch Bureau Detective Squad Recovers Xue Da Shizi 156

Kidnappers Abduct Two-Year-Old Child, Female Kidnapper Captured, Report Submitted for Legal Action

At approximately 7:30 PM yesterday evening, the Zhabei Branch Bureau Detective Squad suddenly received a tip from an informant stating that Xue Da Shizi, a two-year-old nephew of Bian Yingchao, a Funing native who resided at No. 114 Meiyuan Road and was in the trucking business, had been kidnapped by three male and one female kidnapper. Upon receiving the information, Squad Leader Bao Ziying and Chu Jingwu immediately dispatched Deputy Leaders Dong Wenrui and Xie Qihua, and detectives Zhong Da, Mao Gongzhao, Zhang Shuwen, and Zang Nai to intercept the kidnappers. When they reached the Guangzhao Road intersection, the hostage, Xue Da Shizi, had already been taken out by the kidnappers. The female kidnapper had hired a rickshaw and was holding the child, attempting to escape. The detectives, prompted by the informant, approached and apprehended the female kidnapper, recovering the hostage. They noticed several suspicious-looking individuals ahead, who were turning back to look. They sent officers to pursue them. It turned out that those individuals were the kidnappers. Upon seeing the officers pursuing them, they drew guns and fired two shots before scattering and fleeing. The officers escorted the female kidnapper back to the squad and, after a brief interrogation, she admitted to the kidnapping. It was also learned that the kidnappers were hiding in a thatched boat in the river near the Xinqiao of the Shantou Shipyard. Officers were immediately dispatched to arrest them, but the boat had already been abandoned. The Water Police Branch was immediately informed to assist in the investigation. A report was submitted for legal action against the female kidnapper. The hostage was handed over to his family.

This Year's Epidemic Expected to Decrease 157

A Week of Epidemic Prevention Work

The city's epidemic prevention campaign, which began on May 1st, has already been underway for a week. During this week, the first round of vaccinations in the municipal schools in the southern district of Shanghai has been nearly completed. Work has also begun in the Zhabei area, and both concessions are also proceeding.

North and South Municipalities: The Municipal Health Bureau has nearly completed the first round of vaccinations in the municipal schools in the southern district of Shanghai. In the Zhabei area, several schools have already undergone the first round of vaccinations. A total of 15,819 people have been vaccinated within the week: 11,199 males and 4,620 females. It is expected that the work in the urban area will be completed within the week, and vaccinations will be given in rural schools next week. Work in factories and households will begin next month. So far, no epidemics have been detected this year, and it is expected that this year's epidemic will decrease.

Both Concessions: The first round of vaccinations in both concessions is underway. The Public Concession Health Department has dispatched vaccination teams to various schools for vaccinations. However, the effectiveness of each vaccination only lasts for one month, and the epidemic season will last until September. Therefore, the Epidemic Prevention Committee is expected to instruct the health authorities of the concession to continue with the second round of vaccinations in order to achieve complete success. In the French Concession, the French Concession Health Department and the Municipal Health Bureau are working together, with the Municipal Health Bureau vaccination team vaccinating the municipal schools within the concession, and the concession health department vaccinating the private schools. It is expected that all vaccinations will be completed before the summer vacation. As for slums and factories, they will be assigned after the school vaccination work is completed.

Domestically Made Electric Refrigerators 158

Displayed at China National Products Company and Other Stores

Thousands of electric refrigerators are imported into China each year, worth over one million yuan. Most of the refrigerators sold by various foreign firms in Shanghai are American-made, with over a dozen brands. Initially, most of the purchasers were foreigners, but in recent years, an increasing number of Chinese people have been purchasing them. The monthly electricity cost of an electric refrigerator is only three or four yuan, which is not more expensive than using natural or artificial ice. However, the cleanliness, hygiene, convenience, aesthetics, and appropriate temperature control are vastly superior. In this era of global economic recession, various American industries, such as automobile manufacturing, are facing oversupply, but the manufacturing of electric refrigerators is still thriving. Although the use of electric refrigerators in China is limited to urban areas, their popularity has been increasing recently, especially in Shanghai and Nanjing. The Yaguang Manufacturing Company in Shanghai has always been famous in the domestic goods industry for its creation of Bakelite jade products and various electrical appliances. Recently, recognizing the urgent need for self-sufficiency in electric refrigerators, they invested in long-term research and trial manufacturing, and have now completely succeeded. The refrigerator's shell is made entirely of steel, with an enameled interior and a top-quality white paint exterior. The design is very novel, and the interior capacity and shelf area are specially enlarged compared to foreign products to suit Chinese families' needs. There are two models, 5 cubic feet and 6.5 cubic feet. The motor switch is fully automatic and equipped with a temperature controller and an automatic bright lighting system for maximum convenience. Electricity consumption is also very economical. All components have been rigorously tested and are guaranteed to be in perfect working order. The China National Products Company and other major stores in Shanghai are displaying and selling these refrigerators. It is reported that there has been a great deal of interest and purchases in recent days.

French Concession Chinese Ratepayers Association Held a Real Estate Committee Meeting Yesterday 159

Twelve Important Cases Resolved, Paying Attention to the French Municipal Council and Huang Bureau's Appraisal

The French Concession Chinese Ratepayers Association held a joint meeting of directors and supervisors the day before yesterday, resolving to organize a real estate committee. Gong Jingyan was publicly recommended as a member. The committee held its first meeting yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM. Members present included Gong Jingyan, Qu Zhenhua, Gu Wensheng, Zhu Wenqi, etc. Gong Jingyan was publicly elected as chairman, and Tong Lizhang as recorder. After the formal proceedings, the chairman first reported the purpose of the idle meeting and the process of organizing the committee. Then, they began to discuss the work methods and resolved as follows: (1) This committee should solicit members with real estate within the concession to join in order to promote the affairs of the Chinese Ratepayers Association. (2) This committee will conduct real estate registration. The committee will create forms and begin implementation. (3) This committee should issue a declaration and notify the Chinese residents within the concession that property owners should promptly and enthusiastically join the association to protect their own interests and relieve all suffering. (4) This committee should notify relevant Chinese and foreign authorities and organizations of its establishment, stating that any future real estate disputes can be mediated by the committee to facilitate resolution. (5) This committee will hire experts with extensive real estate experience as special committee members to participate in all proceedings. (6) This committee will hire experts with extensive architectural engineering experience as consultants to study and improve Chinese construction methods, reduce construction costs for owners, and lower rents for the benefit of the general public. (7) Regarding the French Municipal Council's recent arbitrary increase in land prices, which has led to increased taxes and affects the livelihood of ordinary residents, this matter should be brought to the attention of the Chinese directors and Chinese committee members, and another meeting should be scheduled to discuss methods to prevent this. (8) Chinese representatives should participate in the (French Municipal Council) Real Estate Appraisal Committee to ensure fair valuation and avoid discrepancies. (9) Establish an investigation office to investigate Chinese real estate and all Chinese immovable property within the concession. This committee will create investigation forms. (10) Restrict Chinese property from being held under the names of foreign merchants. If such facts exist, the committee will not provide protection and will petition the relevant authorities to ban this practice. (11) Regarding the Chinese public announcements issued by the French Municipal Council, the committee will represent a portion of the members who own real estate within the concession to ensure that everyone understands the situation. (12) The current expenses required by this committee will be temporarily advanced by the committee members and reimbursed when public funds are available in the future. After the above cases were resolved and passed, the committee will select and handle them as needed and report the progress to the executive and supervisory committees of the Ratepayers Association for approval and implementation. The meeting adjourned at 5:00 PM.

General Assembly Proposals (A) How should the assembly expand publicity? Resolution: (1) Hold a parade advertisement. (2) Hold a radio broadcast. (3) Tentatively hold a lantern parade on the evening of the 12th of this month. The first two items will be handled by the general assembly office, and the third item will be entirely organized by the general assembly. The performance tickets will be sold by the manufacturers as much as possible, and a lottery will be held to give out prizes, with each ticket eligible for one lottery. Manufacturer Proposals (A) How should the daily business hours be changed and regulated? The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Notice to All Locations After the meeting adjourned, the office immediately notified all manufacturers of the resolutions and added the following note: According to the report of the general assembly police department, it is sometimes discovered that staff members of various manufacturers use Pai Gow and Mahjong for gambling and entertainment. A serious warning is issued. If anyone dares to violate this again, the manager of the factory will be notified to impose punishment, and the police department will conduct a strict investigation.

Last year, Zhejiang Province suffered an unprecedented disaster. At this critical time when the crops are not yet harvested, the disaster victims are in urgent need of relief. Our association is using the national goods movement to implement profit-sharing to promote development, one to promote national goods and resist imports, and one to urgently raise relief funds to help the disaster victims. Since the opening on the 26th of last month, various sectors of the city have come to the meeting to visit and purchase goods, and the response has been quite enthusiastic. Mediation of the Case Against Increased Pig Industry Fees by the Four Meat Guilds 161

No Results Due to the Insistent Attitudes of Both Parties, The Entire Fresh Meat Industry Held a Meeting Yesterday to Discuss Countermeasures

More than 1,000 fresh meat businesses in the Shanghai Public Concession have been in dispute for two months due to their opposition to the extra fees charged by the pig industries in Wusong, and the issue remains unresolved. The various fresh meat guilds are deeply concerned that the situation will escalate, so they convened both parties for mediation the day before yesterday. As a result of the insistence of the industry side, the matter was not resolved. The entire fresh meat industry held another meeting yesterday to discuss countermeasures. The details are recorded below:

Mediation by the Four Guilds Fails

More than 1,000 fresh meat businesses in the Shanghai Public Concession have been affected by the extra fees charged by the pig industries in Wusong, resulting in difficult operations and unbearable burdens. Therefore, they have risen up in opposition and organized an opposition committee to conduct negotiations. Because the industry side has persisted with its views, no progress has been made, so the dispute remains at a standstill. The various fresh meat guilds are deeply concerned that the situation will escalate, so they convened both parties for mediation at Dunrentang in Nanshi at 2:00 PM the day before yesterday (the 6th). More than ten representatives from both sides attended, including Gu Baoxiang from the pig industry and Chen Longhu and Mao Yicheng from the fresh meat industry. First, Fan Deyu, a representative of the guilds, reported the intention of the mediation and advised both sides to make concessions. Then, the industry representative stood up and briefly stated, "The fees charged by our industry are long-standing precedents of decades and are not newly created. The fresh meat industry's request to abolish them all is difficult to comply with. We can only reduce the warehouse fee and store commission by three cents per pig, and a contract must be signed that there will be no objection forever. All the remaining cannot be changed," etc. The fresh meat industry representative then stated that the warehouse fee, store commission, and foot binding fee charged by the industry are unreasonable. Historical precedents have also changed. The old system of the warlord era should be abolished. Because the opinions of both sides were divergent, the mediation could not be established.

The Fresh Meat Industry Held Another Meeting Yesterday

Because the Wusong pig industries persisted with their opinions, the Public Concession's fresh meat industry specially convened a general meeting of representatives of all businesses at 2:00 PM yesterday to discuss countermeasures. More than thirty representatives from various districts attended, including Ju Zusa, Liu Maofang, Wang Liangbao, Yang Yinyou, Sun Hongyang, Wu Wenguang, Ye Shifan, Qiu Shixian, Chen Longhu, and Huang Qixun. First, Chairman Chen Longhu reported on the mediation process of the guild. Then, the following cases were resolved: (1) The Wusong pig industries are only willing to reduce the warehouse fee and store commission by three cents. Should this be accepted? Resolution: We will not rest until the goal of abolishing all fees is achieved. Otherwise, by the Dragon Boat Festival, starting from the January 28th Shanghai Incident, all the fees charged will be deducted from the industry's account and transactions will be stopped. (2) Our industry admitted in a newspaper advertisement last month that it was 3.2 cents per pig. This was due to a misunderstanding at the time. According to Nanshi, it is only 2.3 cents per pig. It should be notified to the Wusong pig industries to handle it the same way as Nanshi. Resolution: Passed. (3) Notice to the industry. Resolution: The secretariat will be responsible for handling it.

Punishment for the Murder Case at the Great World Tea House 163

Li Pansheng, a native of Wuxi, was 44 years old this year. He worked as a food delivery worker at the Dalichun Restaurant downstairs in the Great World building on Avenue Muntigny in the French Concession. At 8:00 PM on the 12th of last month, he entered the Shaoxing opera theater on the third floor of the Great World amusement park to collect bowls. He had an argument with the tea house staff. He was immediately twisted and beaten by Huang Rutang (age 27, native of Ningbo), the tea house accountant of the theater, and three or four other people. Li was kicked in the abdomen and died after ineffective treatment. The French Concession police sent Detective Liu Dianlong to arrest Huang Rutang. Regarding the part of the victim's family requesting compensation for damages, the Dalichun Restaurant and the Great World accountant gave consolation to settle the case. Regarding the criminal complaint, the police sent Huang to the Second Special Court to file a public prosecution on the crime of causing death by injury. The details have been recorded in this newspaper. The case has been completed by Judge Sun Penghan of the Second Special Court. Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, Judge Sun brought the defendant to the court in the First Criminal Court and sentenced Huang Rutang to four years and eight months of imprisonment for causing death by injury. The number of days detained before the verdict is determined will be offset by one day of imprisonment for every two days. During the appeal period, the defendant will be transferred to the detention center to await instructions.

Three Months Imprisonment for Injuring Wife with Scissors 164

Liu Chunhui, a native of Ningbo who used to run a small cigarette and paper shop on Yangshupu Road, closed the shop due to economic difficulties and inability to maintain his livelihood. He often quarreled with his wife, Fang. In November of last year, Fang ran away from her husband and had an affair with a fellow villager named Bao Caisheng, living together at No. 9 Taopeng Road. Liu also often went there to ask his wife for money. At about 1:00 PM on the 30th of last month, he went again for lunch and drank too much alcohol. He demanded 120 yuan as a complete severance of the marital relationship with his wife. Because he did not get his wish, he was very angry. He grabbed a pair of scissors from the table and stabbed her in the eye. She was injured and screamed for help. Chinese Detective Tang Pengfei and Chinese Police No. 2530 from the Yulin Road Police Station arrived, arrested him, took him to the police station, and sent him to the First Special District Court. Because Fang was not present at the Sacred Heart Hospital, he was ordered to send the defendant back to custody and reschedule the hearing after the victim recovered from her injuries. Yesterday morning, Judge Wu Zehan continued the trial in the Third Criminal Court. Li Zhishan, a lawyer from the Public Works Department, stated that Fang's eye injury had slightly improved and that she was present in court to testify. According to Fang, who claimed to be 28 years old, the defendant intended to use scissors to blind her eye and deliberately inflict such poison. If she went home with him, her life would be in danger, and she requested that the court punish him. When questioned, the defendant's confession was evasive. Judge Wu sentenced Liu Chunhui to three months of imprisonment. The number of days detained before the verdict is determined will be offset by one day of imprisonment for every two days.

Feces Rolled Out from the Rupture, Abdomen Injured and Brain Concussion

At about 4:00 PM yesterday, Zhu Yonghe, who lives in Rongfuli, east of Dayang Bridge on Zhongxing Road, Zhabei, and works on road projects such as yellow sand and gravel triplex, had an eleven-year-old daughter, Damao, holding a three-year-old sister, Xiaomao, playing in the middle of the road. Woman Rescued After Jumping into the River 166

Seemed to Be Disappointed in Love

At about 12:00 PM yesterday, a woman who was about 20 years old, wearing a black serge cheongsam and black leather shoes, walked alone to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company wharf on the 16th Pier and boarded a ferry to cross the river. When the ferry reached the middle of the river, the woman suddenly jumped into the river and committed suicide. Her body sank and then floated up. Fortunately, she was rescued by the crew. Because she had inhaled a lot of water, she was quickly sent to the police post at the Pudong ferry terminal and taken to the Pudong Branch Bureau. After being given clothes to change into, the bureau questioned her about her name, age, and origin, but the woman refused to tell the truth. As for the reason for her suicide, she was questioned repeatedly, but she did not reveal it, only saying that she had a relative in the city named Chen Shifan, who lived on Connaught Road and had a telephone at home. The bureau immediately called the place, and there was indeed such a person, but he had not yet returned home. A suicide note was found in the woman's wet clothes, addressed to Tiaohua, which roughly said, "Please wash and dress my body yourself, do not let others do it, and do not use a coffin to bury it, throw it into the sea, this is my last request, you must allow me to do this, from now on we will never meet again, I wish you two happiness and take care of your health, of course." Judging from her tone, it seemed that she was disappointed in love. The bureau also asked if she had been married before, and she replied that she had not yet married. She was first sent to Pudong Hospital for treatment, and her relatives would be notified to come to the case for verification.

Mr. Yu studied overseas and is very economical in engineering and management. Weather Report 179

The Xujiahui Observatory's meteorological forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the weather around Shandong and northern Korea was cloudy with mild cyclones due to the passage and eastward movement of the second low-pressure center. The weather in the Sea of Japan was severe with strong cyclones due to the passage of the low-pressure moving northeastward. The middle and lower reaches of the Yangtze River were cloudy and hot, with southerly to southeasterly breezes and fog in the morning. The East China Sea and the Taiwan Strait were cloudy with gentle and directionless winds. Furthermore, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in the city was 88.7 degrees, and the lowest was 58.5 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 70.7 degrees, and the lowest was 68.7 degrees.

Special Article

Traffic Bank Business Report (XI) 180

4. Future Efforts of the Bank

Due to internal and external difficulties in China's economic affairs, the economic circle and the Bank's efforts to improve the situation have been described above. If we want to see a turnaround from now on, we must make further plans.

China is an agricultural country. The way to save the country is to start with agricultural products. As mentioned above, the essence of rescuing the countryside and supporting production, from the bank's point of view, should be to cultivate its germination and support its growth with various financial methods to make its products find their own way out. In other words, it is to increase its production capacity on the one hand, and to guide it closer to consumption on the other hand, reducing various barriers in the middle. The Bank is responsible for developing the industrial mission, and should recognize this key point of effort as a guideline for business operations. The following is a brief description of the Bank's future efforts:

(1) Continue to promote the Bank in the interior. This year, the Bank has established agencies in the Northwest and Guangdong, which are generally arranged. In the future, we will set up important production areas in the interior, along the new railway lines, and along the open roads, and in the areas where the chaos has been settled. Those who have already been developed will be more closely arranged. Those who have not been developed will be divided into sections and managed in order. The advancement procedures and the density of settings are often determined by the needs and decided at any time.

(2) Really seek closer to the production business. In recent years, the production business has been very depressed, but it is indeed gradually approaching the consumer side. From this point on, we will lead the way and give it a real help. The production business will be able to gradually advance. In the future, we plan to rely on various forms of cooperatives for agricultural products, and provide loans for production and sales to the village. For various industries, we plan to provide various working capital financing for those who can absorb large amounts of domestic raw materials. For the handicrafts of daily necessities, we also plan to select types and give appropriate support to save costs and increase production. Often, different sections are determined, types are determined, and the situation is considered and managed in order.

(3) Support export trade. In order to seek a way out for production, we must guide it to get closer to consumption. On the one hand, we propose to use domestic goods, and on the other hand, we support export trade. We want to provide access to market conditions in various places, plan overseas sales, and offer preferential conditions for export. There are many benefits, so hope is far away. In the future, we plan to expand foreign exchange business in Shanghai, Tianjin, Hong Kong and Xiamen, and set up agency offices in Europe, America and South American business locations, in order to undertake export negotiations as much as possible and support sales. (4) Increase the number of inland warehouses. This year, the number of warehouses has been increased in the mainland, as mentioned above. In the future, we still plan to closely increase the number of sleeves, Jiang Yi in the increase of agricultural warehouses, and its improvement in construction equipment, back to make various domestic production, it is easy to obtain financial financing, when the water line and the freight three categories, examine the needs of the situation, and plan in order.

Education News

Siamese Minister of Education's Sophistry Justifying the Suppression of Chinese Schools 181

Pretending Chinese Schools Violated Laws, Cancelled Compulsory Classes; Did Not Accept the Opinions of Overseas Chinese Representatives

The Siamese government's promulgation of harsh laws restricting overseas Chinese education has aroused public outrage, and people are planning ways to deal with it. The Shanghai Overseas Chinese Federation received a telegram from overseas Chinese in Siam yesterday, reporting that the country's Minister of Education, Pak Son Saraban, summoned representatives of Chinese schools and newspapers in Bangkok a few days ago, to sophistically justify the harsh regulations on overseas Chinese education. Details are as follows:

Publishing an Absurd Statement

On that day, Siamese Minister of Education Pak Son Saraban, accompanied by Deputy Minister and Secretary Nai Wei Tao, met with the representatives. The Minister spoke first, saying that today, we have invited you here to explain the cancellation of compulsory classes. If we describe it verbally, we are afraid that we will not be able to explain it in detail and that we will easily forget something. Therefore, we have issued an explanatory statement today. The reason why the Ministry of Education cancelled compulsory classes this time... After the Minister finished speaking, he distributed the absurd statement to the representatives (the statement is omitted). After the representatives finished reading the statement, the Minister said that all the reasons and answers for the recall of compulsory classes are recorded in the statement, and you should be able to understand it after reading it. (The public did not open their mouths.) The Minister continued, saying that if you have any questions about the statement, you can speak up. So the representatives asked the following questions:

Pretending to Violate Laws to Recall Chinese Schools

(1) A Catholic priest representing the Rose School asked first, "If the Chinese school is run without error and does not violate any regulations, why did the Ministry order it to be suspended and taken back?" (Note: The Rose School is run by Catholics and specializes in teaching the children of overseas Chinese who believe in the religion.) The headmaster replied (hereinafter referred to as "replied" for short), "It is not a question of whether it is wrong or not. The Ministry of Education wants to promote the realization of the educational purpose stipulated in the Constitution, so it ordered the suspension." (2) The Guangzhao representative asked, "Your Excellency said that the Chinese in Siam and running education have greatly benefited Siam, and Chinese schools have shouldered heavy responsibilities for the Ministry of Education for a long time. Now the Ministry of Education has decided to shoulder this heavy responsibility itself. Is this move by the Ministry of Education intended to abandon Chinese schools after they have achieved success?" Replied, "Of course, it has been prepared clearly." (3) Nai Nong, representative of the Siam News, asked (Note: Nai Nong is a Siamese, the principal of Guangzhao School, and sympathetic to the Chinese), "According to the Constitution, people have the right to enjoy elementary education, so let Chinese schools run themselves, which can serve the Ministry of Education, and the results obtained will be the same. Now the Ministry of Education wants to take it back to run it itself. In my opinion, it seems unnecessary." Replied, "Because Chinese schools have failed to comply, they should be taken back." Nai Nong asked again, "If a school does not comply with the regulations, the Ministry of Education can close it, but is it fair to take back all the schools because a part of them violated the law?" Replied, "If not, how can we know that Chinese schools violate the law privately?"

The Number of Unemployed is Bound to Increase Sharply

Nai Nong asked again, "Can the Ministry of Education send staff to manage it?" Replied, "If it is handled like this, the Ministry of Education must increase the number of posts by three times in order to distribute them to the classrooms of each school for management. This is not reasonable." Nai Nong asked again, "In my opinion, the existing staff is sufficient, and there is no need to increase it. As for the results of the management, the students of each Chinese school can be tested at the end of the year. If the management does not have considerable results, the Ministry of Education can also order it to be suspended." Replied, "The questions you have asked are mostly factual questions. These questions have been answered in detail in the statement. As for the Ministry of Education forcibly suspending and taking back the compulsory classes of each Chinese school, the reason is that the Ministry of Education is responsible for the education of children in each Chinese school. There are (1) those who have not reached the age of compulsion, (2) those who have exceeded the age of compulsion, and (3) those who are within the age of compulsion, which is too burdensome. Moreover, the Ministry of Education only takes back the students who are within the age of compulsion to compulsory schools. For students who have not reached the age of compulsory education and those who have exceeded the age of education, I hope that each Chinese school can work for the Ministry." The representative Ren asked, "If so, most Chinese schools will soon be closed down, and most of the staff will be unemployed, and the number of unemployed will inevitably increase. I hope the Ministry will think carefully about this move, which contradicts the major policy of the People's Party." Replied, "No, what the Ministry of Education has implemented is based on the Constitution, and it will not conflict with the Constitution."

Other Foreign Schools are Not Banned

The representative of the Siam News asked again, "Has any other foreign school been ordered to be cancelled this time?" Replied, "When the time comes, they will be cancelled one after another." The representative asked again, "Is this the time or not? In order to make things wait for their peace, they should be cancelled uniformly." Replied, "If so, I need to have four hands and four heads to do it at the same time. At this time, there is only one hand, so only the easy ones are done." At this point, the representatives believed that the Ministry of Education of Siam was trying to cover up its mistakes and had no sincerity in accepting the opinions of the representatives, so they resigned. It is said that they have prepared a book to refute it.

The Ministry of Education Explains the Procedures for Transferring Students 182

The Ministry of Education, according to the Supervisory Office for Students Studying in Japan, submitted a report from Tu Cong, a student from Anhui Province, requesting a transfer and raising questions about the regulations on studying abroad and management. After instructing the Supervisory Office, the Ministry of Education said, "I understand. The student's request for transfer was previously submitted to the Ministry and has been approved and recorded. Publicly funded students studying in Japan who have been studying at the school for more than one year must also be subject to Article 17 of the Regulations on Studying Abroad issued by the Ministry (publicly funded students may not change their subject of study during the study period unless there are special circumstances and the provincial and municipal governments submit a report to the Ministry for approval) and Article 8 of the revised Regulations on Managing Student Affairs in Japan (publicly funded students who have been studying for more than one year may not transfer to another school). However, if it is necessary for this student to transfer to another school to study due to the subject of study determined by the examination, the office may, after investigating and verifying the facts, transfer the letter to the funding agency for verification."

Political News from the Ministry of Education 183

The following is a summary of political news from the Ministry of Education in recent days: (1) The Ministry ordered Tongji University to report the names, qualifications, and positions of foreign teachers. If foreign teachers are to be rehired or newly hired in the next year, they should be submitted for approval in advance. (2) The Qinghai Provincial Department of Education reported that the reorganization of the province's middle schools was approved. However, the teaching subjects and curriculum content of normal schools should be handled in accordance with the normal school curriculum standards, and the examination subjects should be handled in accordance with the regulations on normal school examinations. The Ministry also ordered Fushan Simple Normal School to be reorganized into a vocational school or middle school in accordance with the order. The Ministry of Education Asks for Amendments to the Organizational Law 184

(Nanjing, 8th) The Ministry of Education requested amendments to the organizational law to add four supervisors, two deputy section chiefs, and four staff members. The Legislative Yuan's legal association reviewed the request and decided to amend Article 20 to say that the Ministry of Education should set up six to ten supervisors to inspect and guide national education affairs. The amendment was made to say that the Ministry of Education should set up 14 to 16 section chiefs and 80 to 106 staff members to take charge of various section affairs under the orders of the superiors. The establishment of special secretaries is a common problem in the organization of various ministries and commissions, and it is proposed not to amend it for the time being. The Legislative Yuan's general assembly will pass it on the 10th.

Presidents of Middle Schools in Zhejiang Province Petition to Protect Education Funds 185

The presidents of various provincial middle schools in Zhejiang Province petitioned the government because education funds have been in arrears for a long time, and they were paid at a 90% discount starting in February. On the afternoon of the 7th, more than 20 people, including presidents of provincial middle schools Xiang Dingrong, Fang Hao, and Chen Shimin, went to the provincial government to see Chairman Huang to demand (1) the immediate payment of arrears, (2) exemption from discounts, and (3) protection of education funds. Huang promised that education funds would not be diverted, and the discount on education funds would be repaid when the province's Kang was slightly better. The Finance Department was ordered to allocate the funds for the slightly outstanding months. The presidents of the schools left satisfied.

The Municipal Education Bureau Is Ordered To Hold Higher and General Proficiency Examinations 189

To be completed before the end of July

The Municipal Education Bureau received instructions from the Municipal Government stating that the Examination Yuan plans to hold higher and general examinations this year, and therefore, higher and general proficiency examinations should be held uniformly. This is to allow those with equivalent academic qualifications to participate in the examinations, and those who pass the proficiency examinations will also have the opportunity to participate in the higher or general examinations. Provinces and cities that do not hold general examinations this year should also hold proficiency examinations uniformly, and these proficiency examinations must be completed before the end of July. Upon receiving the order, the bureau is reportedly preparing everything and will request the appointment of a chairman for the examination committee to begin the work.

All Levels of Party Headquarters Promoting Literacy Education Measures 190

The Municipal Party Headquarters issues a notice to all districts to mobilize uniformly, with a deadline of June 20th for preparing and establishing

The Literacy Education Promotion Association organized by the Municipal Party Headquarters regards the literacy campaign as one of the seven major campaigns. All party members should strive to promote it. Special measures have been formulated for party headquarters at all levels to promote literacy education. The Municipal Party Headquarters has issued a notice to all district party headquarters and district branches to take the promotion of literacy education as their central task, with a deadline of June 20th for preparing and establishing. Excerpts from the measures are as follows:

Measures for Party Headquarters at All Levels to Promote Literacy Education 191

Article 1: All district party headquarters and district branches should take the promotion of literacy education as their central task. Article 2: The merit of work performance in each district and branch will be assessed based on the achievement of promoting literacy education. Article 3: Each district party headquarters and district branch in this city should establish at least one literacy school, unless there are special circumstances and approval has been obtained. Article 4: The name and address of the literacy schools established by each district party headquarters and district branch are as follows: 1. Name: Shanghai Special Municipality Party Headquarters, District 〇, Literacy School 〇; 2. Address: If the premises of each district and branch are too narrow or the location is not suitable for literacy education, suitable venues may be found, borrowed, or rented in nearby areas. Article 5: The literacy schools run by each district party headquarters and district branch should designate one person from among the entire committee to be responsible for presiding over it. The teachers may also be comrades with considerable academic qualifications. Article 6: The literacy school should have a term of two months. Each district and branch must run at least one term, and it is even better to continue running them. Article 7: Each class in each school must have at least thirty students. Each school should run at least two classes in the morning and afternoon, with each class lasting at least one hour. Article 8: The person in charge of each department should strive to supervise all comrades to investigate illiterate people and do their best to persuade them to enroll. Article 9: The expenses of the schools established by each department are to be raised by themselves, and no fees may be collected from the people. The books will be issued by the Municipal Party Headquarters. Article 10: The equipment and teaching methods of the literacy schools may be determined according to the circumstances. The people attending the schools should be encouraged in every way to make them happy to learn and avoid dropping out halfway. Article 11: All district and branch literacy schools in the city must be prepared and established before June 20th. Article 12: If a district or branch does not prepare and report within three weeks from the date of receiving the order to prepare, its person in charge will be warned (Executive Committee). Article 13: If a district or branch does not prepare and establish within two weeks from the date of warning, its person in charge will be replaced (Executive Committee). Article 14: Those who have done a good job in running the school and achieved outstanding results will be given medals or certificates of merit by the Municipal Party Headquarters after assessment. Article 15: All comrades in the city with the ability to teach literacy, in addition to serving as teachers in literacy schools, should each teach the people to read. The methods will be determined separately. Article 16: These measures shall be implemented from the date of promulgation by the Municipal Executive Committee.

Automatic Machine Engineering Experts Organizing the Automatic Machine Engineering Society 192

Already approved by the Municipal Party Headquarters, and will be formally established once preparations are completed.

The Chinese Society of Automatic Machine Engineering was initiated in February of this year by Chinese automatic machine engineering experts Zhang Deng-yi, Liang Di-zhong, Huang Shu-pei, and Hu Song-yan, mechanical engineers Wu Qu-fei, Chen Zhuo, Ruan Shen-yi, Li Chong-pu, Zhao Duan-zhang, Ding Zu-ze, Wang Shi-qi, and Chen Shen-wu, as well as automotive engineers and managers Shi Jiu-rong, Shi Jiu-hua, Qian Chong-li, Yu Teng-fang, and Tang Guan-yi, and aviation experts Zhou Huang and Ma Yi-zhou. In accordance with the People's Organization Regulations, they applied to the Shanghai Special Municipality Party Headquarters for approval to establish the society. A founding meeting was held, and Zhang Deng-yi, Li Chong-pu, Ding Zu-ze, Huang Shu-pei, Liang Di-zhong, Hu Song-yan, and Chen Zhong-wu were elected as the seven members of the preparatory committee to begin preparations for everything. All preparations have been completed, and the permit has been issued by the Municipal Party Headquarters last month. The association is reportedly actively drafting the constitution and compiling the list of members to submit to the Municipal Party Headquarters for review. It will be formally established once it is filed.

Ms. Tang Ming-xin Returns Home After Completing Her Studies 194

Ms. Tang Ming-xin, a native of Jiujiang, Jiangxi, graduated from Ginling College in 1928 with a Bachelor of Arts degree. In 1931, she went to the United States and studied in the Department of Sociology at Smith College for one year. In 1933, she obtained a Master of Arts degree in Sociology from Vanderbilt University. Ms. Shi sought further study and wished to conduct a thorough study of applied sociology, and she re-entered the School of Social Service Administration at the University of Chicago for specialized training for a total of two years. She has recently returned to China on the Hoover President at the invitation of Huachung University in Wuchang, and will be taking on the two positions of Professor of Applied Sociology and Director of Women's Affairs at the school starting next semester. It is reported that the subjects studied by Ms. Shi include home economics, childcare, social problems, and social casework, all of which are very novel in China, and will make a significant contribution to the country in the future.

Literacy Education in This City: Jiangwan Experimental Zone Opens School 195

Since the establishment of the Shanghai Municipal Literacy Education Committee in the Jiangwan Experimental Zone, it has begun its investigation. The number of illiterate people has now been fully statistically compiled, and the literacy schools have begun classes on May 6th. Enrollment is still considered enthusiastic. In addition to ordering and instructing Tu and Bao to notify households one by one, those who have failed to enroll on time have been sent letters to the Public Security Bureau to send police to assist in persuading them. It has been found that Director Jiang Wen-shi and clerks Xu Run-jue, Shi Lian-huang, Zheng Bu-hong, etc., of the office are working tirelessly, even on Sundays, and are working as usual. The results in the future are expected to be optimistic.

Moscow Summer Games 202

TASS Moscow, April 6th. The Soviet Union will hold an All-Union Shooting Competition in July and August. Active preparations are underway for the summer games. Commercial News and Finance

Gold Price Continues to Climb to New Heights, Breaking Through the 800 Yuan Mark Again 209

Despite Stable Foreign Exchange, Optimism Remains Strong, Resulting in Another Increase of 9 Yuan and 9 Jiao

The gold market continued to rise yesterday, breaking through the 800 yuan mark. Optimism remains strong, showing no signs of weakening. Although trading in the market was not particularly busy, demand still exceeded supply, and the market situation was very firm. Without special stimulus, it seems difficult to see a decline before the swap period. Earlier in the day, overseas calls indicated that London rose while New York shrank. However, the large speculators' area was weak, and sentiment was unaffected. In addition, the forward silver price in Montr[ea]l fell by 2 to 3 points. The exchange rate opened higher but closed lower. The price of raw gold in London fell by 5 and a half pence. The preliminary trading opened at 96.7 yuan. The trading surface was narrow, and sellers watched from the sidelines, further breaking through the 800 yuan mark, rising to 034 yuan. Large accounts took advantage of the high price to sell, and soon it retreated back into the 800 yuan mark. The Central Bank's official rates were announced, with the British rate remaining flat and the US rate shrinking. The Customs Gold Unit shrank by 5 li, and the standard gold price retreated to 826 yuan and 1 jiao, even lower. However, the price opened high, remaining stable after opening. Later, due to banks cashing out at a high price, the upward trend was blocked and went downstream. Large accounts came to dump again, and the exchange market also hardened due to the banks' selling pressure, once weakening. The exchange rates announced by HSBC Bank remained flat for the British rate and shrank by 0.0625 for the American rate, and then stabilized. Although buying efforts came into play at a low price, due to the banks still supplying, the fluctuations remained uncertain, but generally there was no special change. The psychology of the industry remained good, with repeated short covering. Later, the exchange market gradually tightened, stimulating buying, and finally broke through the 800 yuan mark. At noon, it was even more firm. The situation in the first half of the day remained healthy, but the swap prices for May and June had already fallen back. Yesterday, the short sellers posted 3 yuan, and today the situation in the first half of the day is recorded as follows:

The morning opening was 19.7 yuan, an increase of 5 yuan and 1 jiao compared to the previous close. Dade Chengfu Yu advanced to 8 yuan and 5 jiao, Heng Yu Chun Yuan Yong Shi to 7 yuan. Heng Yu Fusheng Yongfu Yuchang Da Wan Xing Lifeng Laijin rose to 8 yuan and 8 jiao. Maggary [Grindlays] sold July US dollars at 4.375. 杜粳洋米到湧回跌 (The Arrival of 杜粳 Imported Rice Surges Back Down) 219

Yesterday (South Shanghai), a total of more than 50 companies arrived with native rice (totaling more than 10,000 dan), which caused the sentiment to slump and sales to be strangely stagnant. All the rice dealers suspended purchases. At the same time, because the sellers had not been able to sell for a long time, they inevitably panicked and lowered their asking prices to seek sales. As a result, the market tone suddenly softened, and prices of all thick-grained and thin-grained rice fell sharply by 0.20 to 0.30 yuan. However, the noon market recovered slightly after this drop, and the situation seemed bearish. Except for 變元, which did not soften, (North Shanghai) more than 30 boats arrived from the river. All the goods on the market were cleared out. 高貨價 prices of high-quality 开白粳 rice rose by a small fraction of a yuan, and secondary goods also rose by a small amount of just over 0.10 yuan. 薄稻 high-quality goods were stable, and secondary goods saw abundance. Prices of early rice generally fell by 0.10 to 0.20 yuan, and the price of 白元 also fell slightly. The prices of other goods fell more than they rose.

The arrival of imported rice has been constant in recent days, and there are still goods on the way arriving daily. Therefore, merchants and wholesalers are seeking to sell. After a small number of goods on the way were sold off at low prices the night before, all rice prices were weak at yesterday's opening. However, the inland gangs were still able to take advantage of small profits, and the market did not see another crazy drop. However, Saigon No. 3 had already recovered by 0.04 to 0.05 yuan, and other rice had also been reduced by 0.01 to 0.02 yuan. Inland demand is still strong, and Zhejiang needs even more. However, yesterday most were intent on reducing prices for continued purchases, so trading was not as active as in previous days. In the total market, more than 9,000 bags of Saigon spot rice and rice on the way, more than 2,000 bags of 小绞, and more than 5,000 bags of Siamese 暹茄辣地 高贡回範 大绞, etc., were offered. For 客秈 rice, 1,600 bags of Han口 沙市 rough rice were offered, of which, except for more than 1,000 bags of 西贡 going to the local market, all were bought by the inland market.

统牲 (Tongsheng) New Cake Sale Leads to Sales 220

Recently, the soybean cake market conditions have been flat, leading to a softening of the market atmosphere. Yesterday, a Tongsheng relative's factory, due to the new opening, was operating day and night. As a result, the stock of spot cake has accumulated daily. Therefore, they depreciated prices in the market to attract purchases. It is estimated that 15,000 pieces of Four-Brand cake were sold at a price of 1.138 yuan, which were purchased by gangs from inland and Shantou. Other factories were unwilling to sell cheaply, but the buyers were not greedy either, leading to stagnation. Currently, Four-Brand cake is the most sought-after in the soybean cake market, so the prices of other cakes rise or fall accordingly. It is heard that for each cake factory, apart from Dayouyu Factory, all brands above Four-Brand will rise by 0.10 yuan, and all brands below Four-Brand will fall by 0.09 yuan. For other factories, prices must rise by 0.11 yuan or fall by 0.10 yuan.

Silk and Tea 婺休 (Wu Xiu) New Tea 斋帮 (Zhai Gang) Opening 221

The development of new tea in Wuyuan is later than in Xiu, but this year the climate is particularly early. Coupled with the continuous rainy days in the first two sentences, the tea trees in the counties and Zhouyuan gardens are already lush and flourishing. A small number of mountain households in the north townships have advanced the production of Mao Feng. Recently, with clear weather, the tea leaves have been exposed to dew every morning, and the quality has turned from Qingkong to soft and thick. From yesterday onwards, tea gardens in various villages in the four townships have been harvested. The poor see tea mornings in the east township, and most imitate the "tea example," selling zero kilograms. Because tea merchants have suffered losses due to continuous business, they are unwilling to take in tea unless they cut prices. Therefore, although the mountain households want to seek high prices, they cannot. The new spot market yesterday only sold for 0.33 yuan per kilogram, equivalent to 33 yuan per dan, which is lower than last year's mountain price by just over a few yuan. However, in the eighth district of Beixiang Jujian Yuan and the seventh district of Xigu Yuan, the areas with the most abundant tea production, due to rampant bandits, the tea that can be harvested cannot be harvested and produced in time. Both the merchants and the households have not yet opened their gardens and entered the market.

The new tea in Xiuyi County is developing very rapidly. Mountain households in the west have opened their gardens early. Among them, the poor tea farmers have no tea silver to release goods, so they can only produce and sell at will, selling the tea produced daily to the merchants. The merchants also search for and select tender leaves. The new spot market opens at only 0.434 yuan per kilogram, equivalent to about 434 yuan per dan, which is lower than last year's mountain price by more than 20 yuan. The market atmosphere is sluggish, and the mountain households are suffering, which is rare.

Sugar Market 加税 (Tax Increase) is Optimistic for Guangdong Coarse White Sugar 222

Yesterday's sugar market, according to a certain party's message, there is a saying that the tax increase will definitely be implemented on June 1st. Therefore, the market atmosphere and sentiment are both good. The guild divided the market for No. 24 Dutch coarse white spot goods, and the price rose by 0.1 yuan to 16.5 yuan. Re-exported tariffed goods were 5.45 yuan, all of which were traded. The number of sellers was very low, indicating that the future trend is still promising. The Sugar Industry Cooperative Company was scheduled to tender yesterday. Guangdong coarse white sugar was temporarily held due to the optimistic outlook for the tax increase. 1,000 bags of Dutch coarse white sugar were still tendered at 16.7 yuan, which was 0.25 yuan different from the marked price, and of course, could not be traded. Zhenyu No. 1 of this factory's Mian Bai sugar opened at 15.9 yuan, and then called down to 6 yuan. Nos. 2, 3, and 4 were returned as is. Taikoo sugar, today's Mark spot goods, were at 17.3 yuan, and the marked price was short of trading volume, and were still in progress.

North and South Goods 糯米枝 (Glutinous Rice Branches) Re-rise by More than 10 Yuan 223

Glutinous rice branches are the highest quality of dried lychee. Recently, due to both arrivals and inventory being severely low, the base is very scarce, so the trend is suddenly tight, and it has risen by more than 10 yuan. It was found that the previous price was 150 yuan, and yesterday the market had already reached 165 yuan. The next batch of goods from the merchants is said to require 200 yuan. Although no transaction has been made, it shows a glimpse of the tight prices.

生仁 (Raw Peanuts) Market Price Gradually Tightens, Rises Another 0.30 Yuan 224

The price of raw peanuts is gradually tightening because foreign merchants in Qingdao are making moves. Local Guang gangs are very interested in importing. A few days ago, they continued to purchase 40 tons of Guide peanuts at a price of 7 yuan, which is 0.70 yuan higher than the previous market. The market outlook is strong.

Shen Bao National Goods Weekly

What to Eat and What to Read 226

— Yang'an

Nowadays, most people know that vegetables contain many vitamins, so many people like vegetarian food. However, if you carefully check the customs trade books, the vegetables and fruits imported from Japan alone amount to 14 to 15 million yuan each year. Furthermore, if you go to restaurants and eateries to take a look, most of the vegetables and fruits used are imported goods. In this situation, how can the rural areas not go bankrupt? How can wealth not be depleted? The day before yesterday, I went with many old friends to the Shanghai West Farm run by Wang Junzhixin in Caohejing for a meal. I felt that the more than eighty acres of farmland were planted with cauliflower, tomatoes, asparagus, cabbage, coriander, peas, broad beans, and fruits of all kinds. I think this is where the wealth of the rural areas lies. Why don't general restaurants and residents buy domestic vegetables and fruits, but instead use imported goods? Perhaps they still don't know? However, there are many like the Shanghai West Farm, all worried about not having a way to sell their products. Ren Shigang asked me to publish this and introduce it to comrades who love using domestic goods.

Mr. Tianxu Wosheng, recently, in his spare time, has enjoyed writing articles very much. What he likes to talk about most is the issue of paper. I haven't seen him for a long time, but what he always keeps in mind is to solve the problem of paper's outlet. This year is the Student National Goods Year, and it is also the year when everyone is unanimously encouraging young people to read. However, the many books and newspapers that students read are all printed on foreign paper. How wasteful is this? The Promotion Association of Student National Goods Year, because primary school textbooks are mostly printed with foreign paper, conducted an investigation. If domestic paper is used instead, each student will spend an additional two dimes of silver each year on books. They hope that parents are willing to spend an extra two dimes per year for their children to make up for this great regret. This is very meaningful. I think book industry figures such as Wang Yunwu, Lu Feibohong, and Lu Gaoyi must be thinking of a good way to prevent students in the Student National Goods Year from painfully reading materials printed on foreign paper?

### May Ninth and the Promotion of National Goods 227

— Baling

Today is the May Ninth National Humiliation Memorial Day. In other words: "It is the first National Humiliation Memorial Day on which the Republic of China suffered the most vicious treatment from imperialists." When we think back to this day twenty years ago, we can't help but have endless thoughts and indignation! I think that all compatriots of the Republic of China probably share this sentiment!

However, how can we thoroughly redress this extraordinary national humiliation? Some people say: "We must have the whole country, from top to bottom, make concerted efforts, strive for external solutions, and strive for the development and improvement of our own capabilities in order to find a way." Some people say: "We must strengthen our military and prepare for a decisive battle with the imperialists who have invaded us in order to find a way out and escape from death." While we cannot say that these arguments are meaningless or without value, in my humble opinion, promoting national goods is also an effective way to avenge this humiliation. How so? Please listen to my explanation.

We know that the reason why China cannot stand against the great powers can be summed up in one sentence: it is because the country is poor and the people are impoverished. Why has it come to this state of national poverty and popular impoverishment? To put it thoroughly, it is because the Chinese people do not love to use national goods but specialize in using foreign goods, resulting in the outflow of snow-white silver dollars, with hundreds of millions upon hundreds of millions being exported each year, which is a huge fatal blow. Since the founding of the Republic of China, if we carefully calculate the annual trade deficit figures and the silver export figures, the numbers would certainly be extremely alarming! I ask: If a country suffers from the trade deficit and invasion of foreign goods to such an extent, how can it not fall into a state of national poverty and popular impoverishment? Therefore, I deeply feel that promoting national goods is indeed one of the effective ways to avenge our humiliation.

Therefore, I sincerely hope that when the whole country commemorates the May Ninth National Humiliation today, everyone will make a resolution. No matter what field one is in—agriculture, industry, commerce, education, or the military—everyone should establish a belief in using national goods. From now on, whether it is what we eat, wear, live in, or any other item, if there is a national product available, we will absolutely not buy foreign goods. If all compatriots throughout the country have such a concept and such a determination, I can say that within five years, the unemployment problem in the Republic of China will definitely be resolved. The so-called state of national poverty and popular impoverishment in China, which has been covered by great national humiliation for twenty years, will naturally be avenged.

I hope that all beloved compatriots throughout the country will quickly rise up and make efforts! Seize this opportunity of the May Ninth National Humiliation Memorial Day to advance on this path of national goods for national salvation!

My Views on Industrial Control 228

— Hong Fumei

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce believes that Chinese industry has caused overproduction due to the lack of control. Because of overproduction, there is mutual infighting. Because of mutual infighting, everyone perishes together. Therefore, industry is declining and cannot resist foreign goods. Therefore, it has specifically submitted a request to the Executive Yuan to handle industrial control in order to save the situation. This matter concerns the future of the national industry, and we should carefully review it. To say that China, which is regarded by foreigners as the end of dumping and whose industry is extremely immature, is suffering from overproduction is probably not a fact. This is very obvious. Without statistics or investigation, to be alarmed by overproduction seems uneasy.

The reason why national goods cannot compete with foreign goods is that technology, management, organization, equipment, machinery, and other aspects are behind others. The domestic industry also differs in its costs due to the differences in the above-mentioned issues. Costs vary, and prices also rise and fall accordingly. Industrial competition thus arises. As a result of competition, the industry itself is able to strive for improvement, reduce costs, and innovate technology. Thus, the people can use cheap goods to resist foreign goods invisibly. Moreover, survival of the fittest is a natural law. Therefore, controlling industry to avoid overproduction does not seem appropriate for modern China. I fear that the harm will come before the benefits are seen, only giving foreign goods the opportunity to drive straight in.

In my humble opinion, the urgent measures to save the decline of industry are nothing more than the following:

(1) The government should ensure the protection of domestic industries and provide convenience everywhere.

(2) Increase import taxes to prevent the dumping of foreign goods.

(3) Reduce or exempt import taxes on raw materials that are not produced domestically.

(4) Abolish transit taxes and export taxes, as well as various exorbitant taxes.

(5) Encourage exports. For industrial products that are exported, the government should refund the taxes paid on the raw materials or provide special subsidies to encourage them to engage in foreign development.

(6) The government should investigate production and sales, as well as import and export situations, and publish them from time to time so that the national industry can follow suit.

(7) The government should promptly implement trade control and exchange rate management to seek offsetting revenues and expenditures and limit the outflow of useless money in order to stabilize national finances and make domestic industrial development easier.

(8) The government should establish research and improvement institutions to guide the national industry at any time in order to seek technical, management, and other improvements.

(9) Each industry should establish its own goods inspection office to inspect whether the goods have any defects before they are sold. Strictly prevent shoddy manufacturing that hinders the reputation of national goods.

(10) Encourage Chinese people to use national goods. As far as my limited knowledge is concerned, I have written this in a disorganized manner, hoping to provide something for those who care about the domestic industry to discuss.

What Sai Jinhua Said About Mr. Hong Jun 229

— Zhang Mengzhao

— A Small Anecdote of Officials Who Loved National Goods —

During the Boxer Rebellion of the Gengzi year! In the midst of the Eight-Nation Alliance's attack on Beijing, Sai Jinhua, the female heroine who reversed the situation and supported the endangered, in Liu Bannong's "The Story of Sai Jinhua," there is a small anecdote about her husband, Mr. Hong Jun, loving national goods! She said:

"Mr. Hong has been in Europe for a full three years. During these three years, besides handling official duties, he spent almost all his time studying. Mr. Hong is very shrewd, but his temperament is too stubborn. When he arrived in Europe, he refused to use any foreign items at all. He still wore those three-layered 'Fu' character shoes, cloth socks..." and so on.

When I saw that Mr. Hong Jun, as the Qing Dynasty's envoy to Germany, could love national goods in this way, I couldn't help but feel a sense of respect and admiration arise spontaneously! It is especially commendable that he could stand out from the crowd in an environment of Westernization! We cannot dismiss him with a single stroke simply because he was a stubborn feudal figure! As the times have progressed to the present, things have only gotten worse! In the minds of consumers, they think that Western materials are more advanced, and that only by using foreign goods can one be considered fashionable! But the white silver is flowing away! Withered to death! Can you survive alone? According to this argument! We may be able to be careless about other matters, but only by purchasing and using national goods should the public use stubborn habits, unchanging for life! To save our Chinese nation, which is critically ill!

A Glimpse of Visiting the Hongda Art Flower Factory 230

— Gan Chunquan

The Hongda Art Flower Factory is located at Yaojiashiqiao, Zhabei, Shanghai. The distribution address is No. 304 Kangti Road, Beile Road, French Concession. Mr. Hu Rongda is in charge of the engineering, and Mr. Wu Jingshi is in charge of the business. In terms of its business category, it specializes in making art flowers, also known as decalcomania. Art flowers were originally invented in Europe and the United States, and were later imitated by the Japanese and sold to China. The largest portion of its sales is to porcelain shops in Jiangxi Province, used as landscapes, flowers, and figures on porcelain. In addition, sewing machines, wireless radios, phonographs, tennis rackets, bicycles, and spray-painted equipment that are difficult to print trademarks or other color separations on with a printing press can all be pasted with art flowers. They are bright and eye-catching, not easy to peel off, and not easy to counterfeit, so everyone likes to use them.

Engineer Hu Rongda of the factory, in view of the huge outflow of our country's funds every year, studied with great care. Initially, the depth and matching of colors were not uniform and appropriate, and the gold thread used was not bright enough. After several years of practical experience, he finally succeeded and can match foreign goods. The gold trademark on the Shanghai Baonuan vacuum flask is produced by the factory.

The organization of the factory is very simple due to its initial creation, and it is divided into four departments: (1) business, (2) paper making, (3) stone engraving, and (4) machinery. Except for the business department, which is solely responsible for distribution and liaison and is not very relevant to this article and will not be described, in addition: (1) The paper making department has a chemistry room, which specializes in mixing various chemicals to form a paste-like liquid and coating it on paper. It also has a drying room to dry it into chemical paper. (2) The stone engraving department has a drawing room and a stone engraving room, which accepts samples from all walks of life, copies them, and engraves them on the stone. (3) The machinery department receives the completed printing stone frame from the stone engraving department, places it on the machine, and prints various colors on the chemical white paper to make art flower paper, which is transferred to various utensils. Kangyuan Can Manufacturing Factory also manufactures art flowers, which will be described in detail in another article.

Ballad of National Goods 231

— Ji Qian

Let us talk about the past, in those years, the Chinese people did not compete to love their country, the great powers were fighting for supremacy on Earth, our country was weak and it was difficult to stand shoulder to shoulder. Whenever great disasters came, we would sing and dance wildly, and at the same time, greedily purchase foreign goods, causing the country to be weak and the people poor, it was truly pitiful. So much outflow of funds is difficult to calculate, causing people to sigh deeply as if being tortured. That is why the Chinese people advocate Chinese goods, and national goods markets are established everywhere, frequently using words to promote them. It is most hateful that the Chinese people are addicted to foreign goods, ignoring the harms and being greedy for cheapness. They are earning our money to make guns and cannons, and their intentions are as vicious as arsenic. I hope that our compatriots will quickly wake up, and no longer be like fools, drunkards, or sleepers. Commercial competition is the current era, any style is valuable and new, and the people loving their country must compete to be first, knowing that economic aggression is like long guns and cannons stealing people's money. From now on, let us no longer use foreign goods, so as not to donate funds abroad, saving the crisis is right before our eyes!
