"Swearing" and "Implementation" 234

— Rongyu

Tens of thousands of children raise their hands together,

Protecting the family, the country, and the people.

At 3 PM on the 18th of last month, more than 10,000 right hands were raised in the square in front of the Municipal Government; a chorus of voices recited the oath to use national goods. It was tragic, passionate, and unprecedented. This was the swearing-in ceremony held by representatives selected from all the large, medium, and small male and female students in Shanghai to use national goods.

If these more than 10,000 students sincerely persuade their family members and friends, from ten thousand to hundreds of millions, from hundreds of millions to trillions, it is really not a difficult thing. However, I hope that the students who took the oath on that day do not regard the oath as a routine formality. Once the oath is taken, the matter is over, and they can freely buy foreign goods and regard national goods as worthless. Wouldn't this be superfluous?

In ancient times, people believed in divine power, so they regarded oaths as very important. Once a word was spoken, with the testimony of Heaven, Earth, mountains, rivers, the sun, and the moon, they dared not change their minds for the rest of their lives. Therefore, Cao Mo kidnapped Duke Huan of Qi, and Mao Sui kidnapped King of Chu, both demanding that they take a blood oath before letting them go. And these hegemonic rulers who controlled the power of life and death dared not violate their oaths, lest they provoke divine wrath. There are many similar things in history, and I cannot list them all one by one. Now people generally understand that the gods of Heaven, Earth, mountains, rivers, the sun, and the moon do not actually care about these trivial matters; even the city gods and Guanyin, who are worshipped by everyone, only know how to enjoy incense and blood sacrifices, and completely ignore these toothache spells. They may say nice things in their mouths, but in reality, they do exactly the opposite. Therefore, I hope that the students who took the oath on that day will truly act according to the oath. We do not believe in divine power, and we do not believe that violating the oath will bring "divine punishment." However, taking the oath is to express our "determination" and courage. This "determination" and "courage" are not just empty words; we must truly act on them.

"Five-minute maturity." "Forgetfulness." Enemies often use these words to ridicule us. That's right! We have indeed made these mistakes in the past. But from today onwards, especially starting with the students who are known as the intellectual class, let us get rid of these bad habits. Be able to speak and act. Since we have sworn to use national goods, then let us earnestly start using them ourselves and also persuade others to use them.

Tidbits 235

— (Baling)

The tragic May is already upon us! We do not know what feelings our Chinese compatriots have about the arrival of this tragic and miserable May? I think: all compatriots with blood and ambition cannot be unmoved, right?

"Avenging humiliation," "avenging humiliation," cannot be effective by shouting it out or writing it down. The most important thing is that the whole country, from top to bottom, must strive to rise up, seek the improvement and development of their own positions, and jointly use national goods in order to gradually achieve good results.

Everyone considers May to be an "inauspicious month." Some people even say that it is a "poisonous month." However, in my opinion, May can be called a "month of struggle." As long as everyone sees the many national humiliations of China in May and strives to rise up, determined to do something for the country and the nation, isn't May a "month of struggle"? Wonderful Art of Stealing Wine 236

— Shijiu

The "wine" referred to here is "Shaoxing wine." Shaoxing wine is transported and sold everywhere, and it must rely on the Guotang Bank. Let's close our eyes and imagine: a large ship carrying hundreds of jars of wine, including all kinds of Jingzhuang, natural color, Huadiao, etc., wouldn't that make the wine ghosts drool? A generation of boatmen then invented two wonderful arts of stealing wine:

One method of stealing wine is relatively simple, that is, using a long iron pipe, aiming at the wine jar and poking it in the middle of the sealing mud, and sucking it with the mouth; or placing the jar horizontally to allow the wine to leak out. However, this method may sometimes fail, because some jar mouths are sealed with small bamboo leaves, etc., and covered with a dish. This makes the wine thieves unable to use their skills. This spring, I opened two jars of wine, one with only a dish covering the mouth. At that time, I still didn't know what the dish was for, but now I know that it was set up for stealing wine.

There is also a method that relies on a secret medicine. Apply this medicine to the outside of the wine jar, about the size of a cup mouth; to say it a little smaller, perhaps the size of a foreign coin. It is said that after smoking about two cigarettes, the jar material at the application site has loosened, and there are countless sand eyes, and the wine will naturally seep out. After enough wine has been stolen, they gently apply date paste, and the jar becomes seamless again; unless the jar is weighed, no one can see that there is already a problem with it.

Every industry originally has its drawbacks, and it is not only the transportation of wine that is the case. Moreover, stealing wine is still an elegant matter, so it seems that there is no need to blame it deeply. However, in order to prevent fraud, I would like to persuade a generation of wine-loving friends. If you want to entrust Shaoxing wine merchants or friends to transport wine, it is best to weigh it at the Guotang Bank before transporting it to see how heavy it is and record it on the bill of lading; then, you can guarantee that there will be no loss.

Tortoise and Lion 237

— Yu Yi

— After visiting the London Preview —

There is a Mr. "Xinzhen" in Shanghai Tongli who wrote a Yangjingbang bamboo branch poem, saying: "This time, it is shipped to the West, and when it returns, people will look at it with new eyes." Although the words are colloquial, the implication is imaginable.

Indeed, this is beyond imagination, the treasures accumulated over thousands of years will cross the Atlantic Ocean. This is a major event after China's opening up, and also a major event in Chinese cultural history worth writing about.

But after visiting this grand art preview, I couldn't help but think of the categories of Chinese sculptures—the objects near the tortoise and the lion.

The form of the lion represents majesty and power. Now, whether in rural villages or cities, in front of the old-fashioned so-called "gilded world" gates, you can always see a pair of stone-carved lions sitting on stone drums. If it is in Peiping, that is even better, you can also see copper carvings. The appearance is even more magnificent. Seeing these things will make people admire the amazing artistic skills of the time and be surprised that the world despises ancient culture in this way.

As for the tortoise, in the eyes of ancient people, it may have been a kind of spiritual creature with a mysterious meaning, sometimes used to symbolize "longevity, health, and auspiciousness." In ancient times, there were "tortoise shells," "tortoise years," "divine tortoises," and so on. Therefore, in Peiping, outside the palace-style houses, there were often "copper tortoises" and the like placed. Looking at that posture, it is also so proud, with no despicable shape.

Ancient culture was originally static. The tortoise, with its natural thick appearance, is still generous, so it can also be displayed in temples, although the common people feel that it is regarded as a lowly animal.

Therefore, we can say that the tortoise and the lion occupy a considerable position in the temple art. However, this type of object only has sculptures and no paintings, which is quite perplexing.

Motivation 238

Increasing the purchasing power of national goods lies in the improvement of the technology of national goods industries and the improvement of the economic situation.

Small Western Paradise 239

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 13: It's Difficult to Make Wedding Clothes for Others, and It's Pitiful to Sell Oneself; Commodities as Slaves are Also Happy to Go Bankrupt, Speaking of Farmers

When Cheng Zhiqian and Zhou Yourong were talking about the teachers in the Northwest, Wang Beihai, this young man, sighed deeply next to them. Zhou Yourong smiled and said: Before the report, this little brother sighed first, there must be something embarrassing here, so please speak slowly. Wang Beihai said: Before I say it, I want the two gentlemen to understand that the Northwest is a place where even eating is a problem, so where can we talk about education funding? Therefore, the teachers' treatment is meager, and it is not the responsibility of any one party. Zhiqian smiled and said: You child, you can be a journalist in the future. In order to avoid offending people, I will put such a hat on first. So, now that you have a hat, you can speak. Beihai smiled and said: We are talking about primary schools, so let's talk about primary school teachers. Of course, in places with convenient transportation or wealth, the schools will naturally have principals, grade teachers, and the teachers will be adequately prepared. But this is a very small proportion of the entire province, and other than that, everything is possible. The salaries of ordinary primary school teachers are always above thirty yuan. But in the Northwest, there are some very poor counties where primary school teachers cannot earn thirty yuan a year. My relative originally earned eight yuan a month in a primary school in an outlying county, but later, due to insufficient funding, it was reduced to six yuan a month. Because that county seat still had relatively convenient transportation, there were still many people vying for this six-yuan-a-month teacher position. As a result, my relative's job was unstable, and he saw the opportunity to act, bidding farewell to the principal and being transferred from County A to County B. (200)

御香縹緲錄 240

— Originally by Princess Der Ling, translated by Qin Shouou

Now, let's talk about how, on the day the Empress Dowager heard the news that Black Jade had given birth to puppies, she immediately said with delight:

"After the morning court session, we must first go to the dog kennel and take a look at the four newborn puppies."

No matter what the matter, whether it was large or small, as long as the Empress Dowager was interested in it and wanted to do it seriously, it could always be achieved! So, I think even if during the morning court session that day, the ministers brought up important matters concerning the rise and fall of the country, she would certainly not pay attention; unless foreign troops had arrived outside the capital and were about to invade the palace, then she might pay some attention, otherwise, it was absolutely impossible to shift her full attention away from those four newborn puppies. To be honest, at that time, my mind was also completely surrounded by the images of many dogs, and I only hoped that the morning court session would end quickly so that I could hurry to visit that imperial dog kennel. Because before this day, although I had been in the palace for a long time, I had never been to the Empress Dowager's dog kennel. I had then developed a habit of longing to be able to accompany the Empress Dowager every day to see new places that I had not yet visited; especially close to my heart was that every time the Empress Dowager took me to a new place, she would definitely have many interesting things to tell me, which made me feel very satisfied.

We were all standing in the hall, watching the many princes and ministers below the steps, one by one, walking over as usual, chanting their own names, and respectfully kowtowing upwards. (310)

Little Recipes

Lichun Dishes 243

— Fang'an

Lixia is one of the twenty-four solar terms, usually in the fourth month of the lunar calendar. In Tangqi, it is customary to weigh people and burn wild rice, and a few days before Lixia, people must go to the General Cao Temple in Ma'an Mountain to pray for children to be spared from sores and ulcers. These matters related to local customs will be examined and verified later, so I will not elaborate on them for now. However, the so-called "three roasts, five cured, and nine seasonal fresh," I will specifically record them as follows, which are also small recipes for Lixia.

The three roasts are roasted liquor, roasted goose, and roasted sesame cake. Roasted liquor is homemade, not brewed from sorghum, but made from lees, so it is called lees roast, also known as ben roast. It is strong and fragrant. Decades ago, all sauce gardens had to make it themselves, but recently it has gradually been replaced by wheat roast made in Jiangbei. Drinking it on Lixia is said to dispel the steaming air that often occurs in summer and affects the yang organs. Roasted goose is made from fat and tender geese, and it is fragrant and delicious. Roasted sesame cakes are available everywhere, so I will not describe them further.

The five cured are cured fish, cured meat, cured sausage, cured duck, and ash eggs, all of which are made by pickling. The fish and meat are dried and steamed, while the ash eggs are soaked in mud, salt, and brine, sealed in jars, and cooked after a certain period of time. All of these are homemade, made in winter, so they are called cured. However, some are not necessarily made in winter. Some cured meats can even be made overnight. According to Danqian Zonglu, "Cured means evening, made overnight," which is what it means. The taste of salted fish and meat is still fragrant, just like ham and cured meat are wonderful summer delicacies. Ash eggs are also called salted eggs. Although pickled goods shops sell them, they are not as good as homemade ones. Eggs from both chickens and ducks can be made, but duck eggs are better. The best ones have egg yolks that are fire-red, like crab roe. If mixed with aged vinegar, the taste is also like crab.

The name of the nine seasonal fresh has been passed down to this day, but people today cannot fully describe their details. As far as I know, they are loquat, green plum, cherry, black caltrop, broad bean, yellow croaker, garlic, shrimp cake, garden bamboo shoot, etc. Although they have not been completely lost, they cannot be fully said to be the nine seasonal fresh defined by the ancients. Loquat is a famous Tangqi product, with two types: white sand and red sand, and the Yangdun variety is the best. In recent years, the production and sales have been very strong, reaching far and wide. The taste is better than the lychee in Lingnan, but at the time of Lixia, it may not be yellow and blooming on the branches. Green plum is also a local product. Recently, the preserved plum with tangerine peel from Guanshengyuan is also sourced from here. At the time of Lixia, it is just when the green leaves become shady and the fruits fill the branches. Cherry fruits are like red beans, worthy of being a delicacy on the table. Black caltrop is just old caltrop in the swamp, seasonal, but lacks deliciousness. Broad beans are fat at this time. Freshly picked, whether stir-fried or steamed, they are emerald green and lovely, and their color does not change. They are fragrant, waxy, and delicious, and they are a top-grade garden vegetable. Yellow croaker is also known as stonehead fish here. In the past, they were delayed by sea permits, and they were only available in the market in summer, so they were listed as seasonal delicacies. Now, they are available all year round. Garlic is just at its peak at this time, crispy and tender. In addition to being a side dish, it also has the effect of relieving mold. Shrimp cake is made by mixing shrimp with flour and frying it in oil like a cake, so it is called shrimp cake, also known as shrimp ball. Tangqi has always been a water town, and the products of fish and shrimp are particularly abundant. No less than hundreds of thousands of people are engaged in catching shrimp, and the price is very cheap. When they first come out of the water, they are lively and fresh, and no matter how they are cooked, they are fresh and unparalleled, not only the shrimp cakes are good. However, when the shrimp cakes are made, only the whiskers are trimmed, and the carapace is left, so they are exceptionally crispy, truly a delicious snack to accompany wine. Garden bamboo shoot is different from maosun and spring bamboo shoot, because it is produced in farmers' gardens, and it is also just in season at this time.

Lixia dishes also include the so-called "combined scenery," which is to combine shrimp cakes, roasted liver (pork liver wrapped in pork oil and boiled in a pot of oil), crispy sausage (meat stuffing wrapped in bean curd skin and boiled), ash eggs, ham, white belly, etc. in a bowl, which is also a good summer delicacy, especially favored by those who like to drink. However, thirty miles outside of Tangqi, there is no such dish. Only the description is similar to the "All Happiness" dish.

Page 17

Free Talk

"Poetry Talk" 244

— Zhou Shao

After reading Mr. Jiang Jiping's article "On Poetry" published in Free Talk, I found that it had many points in common with my own views. Mr. Jiping is a fan of Yuan Mei, and I also greatly admire Suiyuan. In particular, I like his Poetry Talk. Among the Qing Dynasty poets, although there were many who wrote Poetry Talk, famous ones such as Gong Zhicun's "Beijiang Poetry Talk" and Zhao Yi's "Oubei Poetry Talk", only "Suiyuan Poetry Talk" can be seen to advocate "spirit" and abandon "style", and to promote "humor".

The greatest benefit of "Suiyuan Poetry Talk" is that it is written with a free and easy style, and he never thinks that writing Poetry Talk should be a serious writing about poetry. So people can find in the Poetry Talk discussions about human feelings, jokes, and gossiping. It does not come across as serious. For example, one passage about Wang Yuyang says:

When Mr. Yuyang was the Minister of Justice, he often passed by Ciren Temple. The abbot, someone named Dong, was famous among high officials. Yuyang was quite disdainful of him. One day, Dong complained to him about being busy, probably to show off that he was often invited by princes and nobles. Yuyang did not answer for a long time, and then said solemnly, "Why don't you become a monk?" (I don't have the book at hand, but the general idea is like this.)

This is excellent humorous material, unrelated to poetry, and others would have rejected it. However, he recorded it casually, and we never feel that it is meddlesome.

In fact, what is valuable in Poetry Talk is precisely these kinds of things. If one is simply concerned with criticizing lines of poetry, what taste is left? Furthermore, poetry and prose can never be criticized in the same way. Prose values ​​truth and reality; poetry lies in spirit, in charm, in subtlety, not in style, and even less in word-by-word scrutiny. Xiya said, "When Poetry Talk is written, poetry dies." This saying is indeed true, but only for the general case. A true poetry talk is not impossible. Zhang Ji's poem says: "Maple leaves fall, crows cry, frost fills the sky, river fire, fishing boat, facing sorrow and sleep; outside Gusu city, Hanshan Temple, midnight bell rings to the passenger boat." Ouyang Xiu said that there was no bell sound at midnight, and another Poetry Talk writer argued that there was a bell sound at midnight. What does this kind of thing have to do with "poetry"? Pi Guangye's line says: "Travelers break willows with light catkins, flying swallows abandon mud with fallen flowers." Pei Guangyue said: "Willows should have catkins, swallows may not have mud." (Yuyin Conghua) Another person criticized Du Fu, "Who made you turbid wine? One drunk scatters a thousand sorrows," and said: "Wine was made by Du Kang, and Du Fu did not know it, so how can he be called a poet?" To write Poetry Talk to this extent is truly like Xiya said, "When Poetry Talk is written, poetry dies!"

Poets also like to meddle in other people's business. Suiyuan Poetry Talk says that the more unimportant the matter, the better, so-called blowing ripples in a pool of spring water, what business is it of yours? Yang Tieya tasted willow flowers and said: "Flying into the painted building a few spots of flowers, I don't know whose home the willows are in?" Chen Derong's Qisha poem: "May I ask Half-Lang and Weaver Girl, who crossed the magpie bridge first?" These kinds of things are extremely humorous, but Jiang Shaosheng strongly disagrees. He wrote a debate on Cowherd and Weaver Girl, forcefully saying that there were no such people and no such things. Isn't that ridiculous? I remember when Shaosheng showed his article to Suiyuan, Suiyuan only replied with the words "spoils the fun." This kind of critical attitude is extremely good, and with it to write Poetry Talk, people can keep reading.

Among Qing Dynasty poets, I most admire two people, Wang Yuyang and Yuan Zicai. Yuyang advocated "charm" and Zicai advocated "spirit," which were originally the same path, and their greatest strength was to eliminate the bad habits of poets, never rhyming in sequence, never collecting lines, never linking lines, never stacking rhymes, and never rhyming with ancient people. These five are all major diseases of poets, and being able to eliminate them is not easy. One step further, it is best not to use allusions, but I am afraid that Yuyang and Zicai could not do that!

Mourning (Continued) 245

— Zhen Shi

The bright moon hangs in the clear sky, and the autumn wind rustles through the bamboo forest leaves, chilling people's hearts. I put on my thin silk shirt and held a few mooncakes that my mother gave me. In the deep of night, I walked forlornly, quickly, quickly, the sighing faces of my elderly parents haunting my mind, feeling only desolation, bewilderment, and a suffocating emptiness. That night, you were the only one who accompanied me. We walked side by side, silently, silently, neither of us speaking. But we spoke with silence, ten thousand words, how could we begin to say them? Let the intermittent barking of dogs punctuate the chorus of autumn insects. The vastness of the night, the bright moon, our shadows on the ground, the sand on the road, scraped against our feet with a soft sound. Although that night still had the fragrance of the fields, it was completely devoid of poetry for us at that time.

We walked, silently walking, all the way to the Flying Star Bridge outside the north gate of the city. We had to part, I stopped and tightly clasped your hand, and I burst out the words with all my might:

"Second brother! I don't know when I can return to our hometown again... What are your plans for the future?"

You did not speak for a long time at that time, your eyes fixed on me, then you said in a hoarse voice:

"I can't say for sure what will happen? But I must go out, I can't stay in this house."...

From that night on, I began to wander. Because of the torment of life, I was unwilling to write many letters home, and you would not know where I was. We have not exchanged letters for four years. In the autumn of 1931, I learned some news about you from a visitor from my hometown, which made me unspeakably happy, and at the same time, unspeakably ashamed. But soon after, you died, and my mother also died. How can I cry for your death? I can only comfort your spirit with anger! To warm my soul. For the true love and peace of mankind, for the vengeance of the devils, I am angry, facing all the ugliness in this world.

Interest 246

— Feng Zi

Sheng Shumeng criticized Andreyev, saying: "Looking at Andreyev's works over the past twenty years, except for a very few, they all touch on social issues." He also said: "To understand Andreyev while ignoring society is like studying smoke while ignoring fire."

This statement is very accurate.

Although Andreyev once estimated everything with a pessimistic and negative eye, his works have mostly not deviated from society, which is an undeniable fact. Such a popular writer—if he must be regarded as a popular writer—whose works are not understood by the general public is inevitable.

All realistic depictions linked to social issues, to the general public, are not very interesting.

They completely read novels and do literature to find happiness, so the focus is on interest. Their interests are: the joys and sorrows of talented scholars and beautiful women, the strange behaviors and quirks of high officials and nobles, children born with three feet, monks who live to be two hundred and sixty years old, the smiles of courtesans, the thighs of dancing queens, white light spewing from nostrils, chivalrous people chasing and killing, and bizarre blood cases, strange customs, etc., all of which make them feel interesting and fun.

This is why Savage Notes have been published in ten volumes, and Conan Doyle has finally been able to have a broad audience.

However, if the above-mentioned kind of interest is transplanted into the more serious so-called pure literature, the result, I think, will not be good, and it will make readers have no intention to find the true meaning of the article. If the toxic elements are removed, then the interest of the general public will also be removed.

What remains is still only pure literature that cannot gain a wide audience.

Therefore, it is absolutely certain and unquestionable that more interest needs to be added to the more serious so-called pure literature. However, to remove the toxic elements while still retaining the interest is a difficult task, at least in our society.

If we want readers to be able to appreciate pure literature and understand true interest, we must liberate them from toxic, low-level interests. April 20th.

Street 247

— Xi Jun

Skyscraper-high three-dimensional buildings, standing one after another on both sides, are the bones of the street. The arteries of the street, however, are strings of streetcars, rows of cars, and the rows of people, and these interwoven scenes constitute the complex content of the street. The things carried on the street are mostly noisy, except for lifeless houses and other still objects. What the street leaves in your memory is an incoherent agglomeration of clamorous cries and crude mixed sounds, impressions. The scene of the street is discordant and ugly. The tricycle drivers and beggars are cumbersome parasites on the street, like sores and scars on a person's body, but they can't be removed no matter what, and they are always breeding everywhere.

Gentlemen walking down the street arm-in-arm with noble women suddenly have a dirty hand thrust out from the side begging for alms, snot and tears mixed together running all over the face, following them and making a whining sound. This cannot but be regarded as the biggest shortcoming of an elegant street, but there are even bigger shortcomings! On the street at night, in the dazzling bright light, under people's prickly eyelids, groups of women with heavy rouge on their faces and perfume all over their bodies, whose livelihoods depend on selling their own bodies, are arranged smiling on the street. Like butterflies shuttling through the crowds, throwing seductive smiles, wicked eyeballs, and soliciting the flow of people.

This is an even bigger black spot on the beautiful street. The street is indeed too wretched. People may also think that these shameless people have made the street unbearable, but on the other side of the street, on the high foreign-style buildings, women wriggling in the rhythm of jazz music, whose bodies are also like commodities, feel that they can be intoxicated and intimate when they are auctioned off, and they are happy to spend money to exchange for embracing relationships. Yes, the street exists in such contradictions, thriving day by day, with new tall buildings being produced in unlimited quantities, and new shortcomings also continuing to expand at the same time. More and more people are making a living on the street by selling laughter.

Because everything on the street waxes and wanes together. Some things are produced, and some things are naturally consumed. The street was lively before, and it is still lively now, but it has added a lot of new tricks. Countless large cloth advertisements for year-round sales are always floating in the air. On the street, there are storefronts posting signs saying they are closing down every day. This kind of thing was rarely seen on the street in the past, but now it has become the most eye-catching ornament on the street.

The street was originally static and unchanging, but the things carried on the street are gradually changing. Some are increasing, and some are disappearing.

Assahan Miscellany 248

— Fei Er

"Singapore" is next to the pier of Asahan. In the customs, the two Chinese novels that I brought for entertainment on the journey were entangled by the customs officers. Thanks to Mr. Lin's proficiency in Malay, he explained to the customs officers that these were for travel entertainment: "This is for 'fun', it doesn't mean anything." And we transferred from a neighboring port in the Dutch territory, not newly imported from another country. As a result, we were allowed to pass.

"The Dutch territory is not very unified in its administration due to its geography and history," Mr. Lin said to me after we left the customs: "So even bringing books on a journey is troublesome and risky." He added:

"It's best not to bring them."

I could only nod in silence. What could I say to the colonial subjects of the East?

After entering the hotel and taking a shower, we went to a Hainanese restaurant nearby for dinner.

Although there were not many people in the restaurant, it was very noisy. In particular, two elderly Chinese immigrants at the next table, discussing the domestic situation in Malay, were deafening. They seemed to not speak Chinese at all (this was proven after my investigation), but they were extremely concerned about national affairs. It could be seen from the fact that they were arguing about the outcome of the debate, with white foam hanging on their mouths, even to the point of fighting. I knew that since the National Revolution, the overseas Chinese community had been greatly stirred up. Seeing that even the Chinese immigrants who had already become Malayized were concerned about national affairs, it gave people great hope for the future of the nation. However, after that, what else aroused interest besides using Malay to argue about the outcome of the debate?

After dinner, Mr. Lin accompanied me on a tour of the streets of Asahan. The "Pasar (market)," which had once caused conflicts between the Chinese and Malay people, attracted my attention even more. The "Pasar" here has a characteristic, which is that it is full of Malay people: and is quite different from other places where it is almost entirely monopolized by the Chinese.

"The Malay people here are very rampant," Mr. Lin told me: "Some time ago, in order to compete for the sales rights in the 'Pasar,' it caused Malay people to boycott and fight the Chinese. Later, the Dutch government secretly incited and encouraged this matter, but then used force to stop it. So far, the Chinese in Asahan have conceded in the 'Pasar.' Just imagine, if the Malay people everywhere were so stubborn, not to mention that the Chinese would suffer, even the rule of the white people would be difficult!"

I listened silently, without saying anything. I thought that the Chinese people's "sandwiched" position was pitiful and shameful. The Chinese and Malay people, who are both oppressed, why can't they unite harmoniously? Why do they have to fight each other? Isn't this exactly what imperialism hopes for?

"Since that incident," Mr. Lin continued, "the Chinese have given up the sales rights in the 'Pasar.' And the colonial government, seeing that this incited anti-Chinese trend would turn into shaking their own rule, used force and mediation to suppress the incident. Now, the Chinese are prepared for the Malay people here, and the unity of the Malay people here is also stronger than that of the natives in other places. So the Malay people's anti-Chinese sentiment may be incited again.

I eagerly asked:

"So, since that time, has the trend ever broken out again?" (To be continued)

— TK

Beyond the rugged road lies a beautiful land

Three Days (6) 249

— Luo Hong

The rain still hadn’t stopped, and the northeast wind brought with it a dampness that permeated everything. Looking at the sky, it seemed it wouldn't clear up anytime soon. Huang Zhongpu carried two heavy rain boots, walking on the muddy road, his body swaying precariously, often on the verge of falling. But on the wet, muddy ground, he could vaguely see Youfa’s pitiful face, as if begging him: "Mr. Huang, please have pity on me, please go and discuss it with Master Lu, ask him to show some compassion and lend us that money. The Longhui money is only due in three days!" At those moments, Huang Zhongpu would definitely hum in his nose, showing them a bit of his power, letting them know how formidable Huang Zhongpu was. In this village, he was the one with the most face in front of Master Lu; there was no one else. He also had to teach Youfa a lesson, that ignorant fellow Youcai needed some discipline; so young and yet so stubbornly unyielding. In the end, he’d suffer losses that wouldn't be worth it. At this moment, Youfa’s pitiful appearance must be quite amusing. He would deliberately say that three days was too short and the matter might be difficult. Master Lu’s money wasn’t readily available at home. He’d keep saying this until, with great difficulty, he finally agreed to handle the matter, but only if Youcai’s wife immediately entered the Lu household as a wet nurse.

He walked triumphantly on the muddy road, laughing in his heart at the thought. Just as he crossed the narrow plank bridge, he saw Youcai and Hu Yongliang and a few others standing by the tofu shop. Hu Yongliang was mumbling something. Youfa’s high cheekbones and square face struck him like a blow, making him tremble violently. Youfa’s pitiful shadow disappeared to who knows where.

"Mr. Huang, why are you missing a tooth? Did Master Lu…" A young man beside Hu Yongliang said, and then burst into laughter.

Youcai also laughed crisply.

Huang Zhongpu quickly licked the gap in his upper row of teeth with his tongue. A dozen eyes were fixed on him. He didn’t have time to hum at them dismissively. Afraid of being held up, he hurriedly walked past.

You little brats, don’t be so unrestrained. See if you’ll have a good outcome! Youcai, you monkey, don’t… there are still three days, three days…

Huang Zhongpu grumbled this in his stomach. He was sure that these youngsters would come to no good end and would be severely punished as bandits by the county. He quickened his pace. He would go to the head of his bao (neighborhood watch) and make sure the bao chief urged them to pay up quickly. There were only these three days; not a single day could they be allowed to relax. (End)

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Commentary

Banning the Welcoming of Gods and Temple Fairs 250

— Xing An

Following the Kalachakra Dharma Assembly, the welcoming of gods and temple fairs have sprung up in various localities throughout our society. Not to mention distant events, but recently, there was a welcoming of gods in Pudong followed by a temple fair in Jiangwan. This echoed throughout the city, driving everyone wild with excitement. Recently, I heard that residents of Zhabei, not wanting to be outdone, are also brewing something similar. As long as the funds are available and the authorities don't prohibit it, the grand occasion will not be less than that of Pudong and Jiangwan.

However, it is extremely unfortunate that during the welcoming of gods and temple fair held in Jiangwan the other day, an incident unexpectedly occurred where a member of the fire brigade burned down a statue of a god. The fire brigade member's action was intended to break superstition, and it gladdened the hearts of the people. However, this matter has aroused the anger of the local people. Merchants have petitioned the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to uphold justice and to suspend the subsidy to the Jiangwan Fire Brigade. On the citizen's side, the destruction of the god statue has caused deep grief, and people are wearing black gauze armbands to express their mourning. They are also demanding that those who burned the god statue restore it to its original condition to appease public anger. The depth of superstition among the ignorant Chinese people is evident.

Welcoming gods and temple fairs are superstitious practices that waste manpower and money, providing no real benefit and causing harm. It is only because the Chinese people have always been deeply superstitious, and because of corrupt and outdated customs, that such foolish actions occur from time to time. And the authorities, in order to accommodate the psychology of the people, do not stop them, so this trend continues to this day, and even becomes more intense.

Recently, the Municipal Party Headquarters stated that the welcoming of gods and temple fairs in various places in the city is very prevalent, which not only violates the prohibitions, but also harms social order. Moreover, Shanghai is regarded as a place of observation by both Chinese and foreigners, and a source of cultural guidance. What is heard there is followed by the whole country. At a time when the New Life Movement is being actively carried out, the holding of these welcoming of gods and temple fairs may cause foreigners to suspect that our so-called New Life Movement is mostly like this. Therefore, it has specially sent a letter to the Municipal Government requesting that it issue a prompt announcement and strictly order the Public Security Bureau to take responsibility for banning them. This will undoubtedly be of some benefit to national rejuvenation. Luo Jia

A Strange Traveler at the Bottom of Tanzi Bay 251

— Luo Jia

(I am afraid of the authority of fate!)

In dreamlike emotions, I often float like a drifting ship in the lonely sea of people, wasting my unrecoverable youth so carelessly.

— Is wandering to forever restrict the brilliance of my life?

I ask this question, but no one answers it for me. I can only expect my own answer! However, I will never have an answer. Yes, my little boat of life sails in the stormy sea, and my boat lacks the rudder of life. How then will I answer my own question?

(In my small room, you will not find a calendar, because it is most likely to cause my sighs.)

I spend my days in a long nightmare, as easily as smoking a cigarette. Moreover, I am often moved east and west by modern transportation tools. I believe that my travels are not as accurate as the migration of migratory birds! However, I have no definite plan.

After spending the winter in a small mountain town, I came to this bustling seaside city with the spring. This is the second time I have used the muddy water of the Huangpu River for drinking.

The baton of fate drives me to enter the impoverished Tanzi Bay. I became a strange traveler at the bottom of Tanzi Bay without a specific destination.

(I should tell you: my residence is a small box with a small window on the east side, made of broken tinplate. The four walls of my small room are like original cardboard. Dust and cobwebs fill the corners. Don't be surprised. In Tanzi Bay, my small room is like a twenty-four-story building. Looking out from the small window, there are rows of thatched sheds. These houses are inhabited by families of manual laborers! Their souls are kind. You will believe my words, right!)

Every morning, the factory sirens respond to each other like madmen. They drag my soul back from dreams. Then, I jump out of bed and begin the day. This is how I finally settled down! The entire shape of Tanzi Bay, the faces of the residents of Tanzi Bay, and all their lifestyles are a bit too unfamiliar to me!

However, I am willing to slowly get to know them. I cannot bear the strange looks that Tanzi Bay throws at me. This is an insult to me.

(Isn't it? I am only wearing a worn-out blue cotton robe and walking on the small street back to my residence, but I see a group of ragged children casting mocking glances, making me feel for no reason that I am living in an environment where people do not understand each other. Yes! The people of Tanzi Bay despise long clothes. They believe that manual labor is the greatest, so they wear short clothes. The group of short-clothed people cannot tolerate a long-clothed person!)

Therefore, I carefully abandoned my inherent notions and began to observe the depths of the souls of Tanzi Bay. From its side profile, from its cross-section, I should understand Tanzi Bay. I believe that if Tanzi Bay is to understand me, it must first be through me understanding it.

As a result, I gradually understood Tanzi Bay. The name of the strange traveler at the bottom of Tanzi Bay has become a gracious epithet for my past life!

The Heaviest Burden! 252

Wayside 253

— Hu Weixiong

Reaching the river dock, the small steamer had already sounded its horn for the third time. The porter carrying my luggage told me my cabin number. I said goodbye to my little brother and boarded the steamer. Because it was spring, merchants who had returned home for the New Year were now leaving their hometowns again. The small passenger cabin was crowded with passengers. I stood at the bow of the ship and waved to my little brother twice. The ship slowly pulled away from the shore. I watched my little companion holding the porter's hand—his figure disappearing into the pine forest—before squeezing into the cabin.

The water journey here is twenty li, and the small steamer makes a round trip once a day. Land travel is impossible. However, this small steamer often doesn't run for several days for lack of passengers. When I came from there, it was winter, and the cabin was just as crowded. They were carrying the fruits of their year-long hard work, returning to the warm "home" at the end of the year to enjoy family happiness. I had gained a three-month unexpected vacation to recuperate in the mountains. Wasn't a kind of joyful delight the same for both of us?

It was like a son who had fallen into a foreign land, once returning home, being caressed by motherly love—the moving hospitality of a friend's mother, and the companionship of my little friend alleviating my loneliness—one hundred days of life allowed the wounds in my blood to melt in the warmth of this cozy nest. I myself am a homeless wanderer, vaguely recalling the golden age of childhood in my dim memories. But these imagined joys are shattered like waves by the reality of life. Three months of cohabitation have rekindled my dim warmth. But now, I am being taken back to the cruel world by this small steamer! So I closed my eyes, as if trying to ward off the arrival of all unpleasant attacks, and slumped on the deck, isolating the world from myself.

I listened silently to the sound of the ship cutting through the water, loudly splattering as the engine churned. Sometimes, it seemed to roar as if unable to bear the pressure. Involuntarily, I opened my eyes to survey this real world: there were old men with long white beards hanging down, women with mournful faces, school-aged children who should be enjoying higher education, and perhaps others like me, homeless people. These people all had to complete the thirty-li water journey before flying off in various directions. "Why?" I asked myself. The splattering sound of the water answered me.

Unfortunately, I didn't pay attention to the passengers on the steamer coming here. When they were flying back to their warm nests, drunk on a joyful dream, perhaps they had cast all their pain behind them. But they had already anticipated the day when the steamer would carry them back out. "What is this for?" Is happiness and pain relative, or is happiness hidden behind pain?

The sound of the water at the stern of the ship grew louder. I glanced out the window. The small steamer had entered the official river. Orienting myself, I saw we were passing the Filial Daughter Temple. The scenery along the shore was familiar, like old acquaintances. It was as if I had jumped into a small boat, and the boatman was eagerly rowing, reaching the river dock of the Filial Daughter Temple. Isn't that the red wall of the Filial Daughter Temple, reflecting the brilliant sunlight? Aren't those the chimes coming, the morning chanting of the monks from the Filial Daughter Temple? Although the image of the Filial Daughter Temple initially shattered all the pleasant feelings of being secluded and otherworldly, the monks in the Filial Daughter Temple were all homeless people, just like the travelers on the steamer. They put on a serious face and didn't try to take money from the donors. This is not a crime; this is their strategy for survival. In the world around us, there are many who use improper means to deprive others of their right to exist!

Watching the Filial Daughter Temple fade away on the starboard side, I felt that a poignant story was hidden here! I felt that this red wall was lovely, I felt that this chanting was melodious. Yes, everything in the mountains is lovely. But this small steamer, with its splattering water sound, is heading in the opposite direction.

Hotel 254

— Jing Yun

The sun, as big as a large bronze gong, with its egg-yolk-like color, finished its journey, and with a tired body, lazily drilled behind the rubber plantation to the west.

The heat on the earth had gradually dissipated. A gust of cool wind, light and clear, leaked from the tops of the rubber trees, kissing people's bodies and minds, as refreshing and cool as having eaten a cup of ice cream, making people forget the labor and heat of the day.

At this time, Yongxing Toujia, with his bulging belly, stood at the door of his hotel, facing the light evening breeze, leisurely and relaxed, watching the scaly red clouds in the blue sky and the tired crows returning to the forest, waiting for customers coming out of the rubber plantation.

Yongxing Toujia’s hotel was located on the right side of the rubber plantation, on a gentle slope about a dozen steps away from the rubber plantation. The scale of the shop was not large. The low-lying attap roof house was furnished with a dozen old and dilapidated tables. A row of "white wine" bottles was displayed high next to the counter, and some inexpensive snacks to go with the wine were placed on the counter, such as sardines, dried fish, green beans, and assorted salted pickles. His customers were those workers who came out of the rubber forest, their bodies dripping with foul sweat, and their faces as black as charcoal. Besides them, it was rare to see a passing stranger walking into his shop to drink three or five cups throughout the year.

When the sun reined in the power of its scorching flames every day, lazily hanging like an egg yolk on the top of the rubber trees, Yongxing Toujia would show a triumphant smile, standing at the door of his hotel, as if welcoming guests. Naturally, this was the time when the workers in the rubber plantation finished work. At the same time, his hotel’s business was just starting to get lively and energetic following the time when the workers in the plantation finished work.

"Ha, Mr. Kun Mengde, why haven't you come to my little shop for a few cups in the past few days? You must be very busy with 'life' recently…" Yongxing Toujia saw the foreman Kun Mengde, whose whole body was as black as charcoal and covered in needle-like tattoos, staggering out of the forest gate. He rushed

Page 21

forward, grabbing his thick arm, and said in broken "foreign language". "Why, you look a little thinner after not seeing you for a few days, your complexion is really terrible, could it be that you can't sleep well at night? …Hehe!…"

The man called Kun Mengde seemed to ignore him, lowered his head, his heart seemed to be full of all kinds of worries, and slowly followed Yongxing Toujia into the hotel.

"Afu, get half a catty of 'white wine' for Mr. Kun Mengde, and a plate of dried fish… choose the fresh, big ones." After Yongxing Toujia ordered the shop assistant, he approached Kun Mengde's table and sat down. "This dried fish just arrived from Ganggu today, it's big and fresh, very suitable for your taste, Mr. Kun Mengde, I guarantee you won't want to leave after eating it." Yongxing Toujia said flatteringly, he knew that this man liked to eat dried fish the most.

"Uh…" that person casually grunted in his mouth, then remained silent like a wooden puppet.

"Mr. Kun Mengde, could it be that you got angry with your family today, why are you so unhappy?" Yongxing Toujia knew very well that Kun Mengde was an extremely cheerful person. Jokes from his mouth were like the flowing water in the Chao Phraya River, gushing endlessly. But such a silent attitude today was something that Yongxing Toujia had never seen in the twenty-odd years he had known him. As a result, Yongxing Toujia also felt a little uneasy.

"Yongxing Toujia, I'm afraid your business won't last long…" After a while, Kun Mengde finally opened his mouth, stretching his hoarse voice as if with great effort. "The 'boss' of the rubber plantation doesn't want to do this business anymore… you know, the rubber business has been losing money severely for the past few years, putting his thousands of dollars of family property into it. Now, 'Shanding' is strictly restricting rubber exports, causing a lot of rubber to be unsellable and piled up in the warehouse. But recently, they are going to levy some kind of 'business tax', which really makes the 'boss' feel disheartened—now, the 'boss' has decided to close down the rubber plantation in the near future…" He filled a cup of "white wine" and gulped it down his throat with a "gulp," then poured another cup.

Yongxing Toujia was a little dazed at this time. His head felt heavy and dizzy as if he were drunk, and his eyes stared motionlessly at Kun Mengde's red eyes, unable to say a word. His heart was tightly entangled in a web of worries. He thought: "After the rubber plantation closes, where will this hotel—the hotel that supports my family—relocate to?"

When Flowers Fall 255

— Wei Mang

When flowers fall, spring has returned!

With a sense of despondency and disillusionment, I stand forlornly before the lonely peach tree.

Am I dreaming of the spring that has passed? Spring has returned!

Is spring the mystery of youth, the dream of humanity? In spring, the heart of youth is overwhelmed with pain. But when spring leaves, and the falling red turns to mud, the heart of youth aches as if it has been stabbed!

— Spring, the season of love; when spring leaves, love also leaves with it!

Thinking of the past, how can I not shed tears of sorrow?

A time of light sorrow and vexing falling flowers!

Life 256

— Rui Zhi

The slight wind in the spring night, blowing across a flushed face with a hint of alcohol, sweeps across this midnight road. Piercing through thousands of pores, it feels as cool as if it were blowing from an air conditioner. The hot air, filled with a strong smell, that escapes from the mouth, rushes into the nostrils with the light wind. The waves of unbearable alcohol press so hard that even breathing feels stifled and painful.

Tired and dazed eyes are slightly open, and everything in sight seems to be dancing a quick waltz, spinning. The head already feels uncomfortably heavy. However, in the chaotic vision, although the magnificent and luxurious hall has disappeared, and the scene of red lights and green shadows has vanished, her face, an oval one that is already haggard, still flickers on and off in the eyelids.

Before two o'clock, as soon as I entered that magnificent and luxurious hall, Mu discovered her sitting in that row of women’s seats. When Mu told me, I suddenly felt a tightening in my head, and the blood flow seemed to be stung by the sound of gunfire, spinning rapidly. I didn't dare to look at her, but her haggard face had already been deeply imprinted in my mind. Her phantom, which had been fading in my memory, intensified its power and threatened my nerves. I was completely immersed in the dream scene of deep thought.

It was a year ago! It was a summer evening, and the stuffy air oppressed my breathing. In the middle of the night, I suddenly woke up. Everything on earth was immersed in a sea of stillness. The house was pitch black, and the dim yellow light from the gas lamp at the corner of the alley seemed exceptionally bright at that time. I leaned against the window, peering out at the urban scene in the dark night. Suddenly, the face of a young woman appeared before my eyes. She lived opposite my window. At that time, she was already very tired from returning from that magnificent hall.

Since that night, she had caught my attention. I was trying hard to find out her background and name. This motive for curious inquiry arose because I discovered that she was still working hard to study when she was resting. I really wanted to understand, since she was already an unfortunate woman in the city, spending her life all night in that luxurious and magnificent den of exchanging wine and meat, what kind of mood could she still have to work hard?

However, my curiosity finally disappointed me. Before finding out, I had already left that house. From then on, I had no longer seen her, and her image had gradually faded in my memory and was about to disappear.

But tonight, she appeared before my eyes again. Her impression on me was emphasized again in my mind. However, tonight she was not the her of a year ago, not the life of an unfortunate woman that I wanted to inquire about. However, the impression she gave me tonight was deeper than before. From her face, I could see that she was haggard because of life.

Movie News

Grand Opening Ceremony of Cultural Film Company 260

The up-and-coming Cultural Film Company held its opening ceremony at midnight yesterday. About two to three hundred people from all walks of life participated in the company's opening ceremony. Celebrities in Shanghai such as Du Yuesheng, Zhang Xiaolin, Wang Xiaolai, Chen Yonglin, and Zhang Weiru also participated. The first scene filmed that night was a stage scene, namely the "Jiangnan Drought Relief Entertainment Gala" in the play. In order to be realistic in the play, Mr. Wang Xiaolai was invited to give a speech, and Mr. Cai Diaotu, a reporter from the Social Evening News, was responsible for recording. Mr. Wang Xiaolai's speech was very poignant and moving. Mr. Wang Xiaolai said: "Floods occur in one line, droughts occur everywhere, so droughts are actually more harmful than floods... To be honest, the compatriots in the disaster areas now have no clothes or food, and are suffering from hunger and cold. Please, gentlemen, transfer the cost of smoking cigarettes to help the victims..." Everyone who heard this was moved.

After Mr. Wang Xiaolai's speech, the company's debut work, "Parents and Children," the first program of the entertainment gala in the play, "Ten Thousand Taels of Gold," was filmed. The richness of the stage scene in "Ten Thousand Taels of Gold" is rare in domestic films. The singers and dancers performing in the play have undergone long-term training before filming, so the various dance postures performed are extremely exquisite and unparalleled. It is said that the dance was taught by a famous European dancer, and the accompaniment was also by a famous foreign orchestra in Shanghai. The lead actress is the nationally renowned singer and dance star Gong Qiuxia.

"Grace of a Beauty" Successfully Completed 261

"Grace of a Beauty" is a famous work by Zhang Henshui. Tianyi Company put it on the screen, directed by Wen Yimin, starring Lu Lixia, Li Ying, Wei Pengfei, Zhang Zhenduo, Shen Yalen, Zhao Xiaofo, Xiao Zhengzhong, Tian Taixuan and other male and female stars. In addition, there are dozens of first-class singers from the "Mingyue" and "Xinhua" dance troupes, Bai Hong, Li Mingjian, Yan Fei, Zhou Xuan, and Xu Jian participating in the performance, which is the perfect combination and like icing on the cake.

The film was shot two months ago, but because of the insertion of subtitles, the addition of music and singing, the work was extremely complicated, so it was not until recently that all the merits were completed. It is expected that it will be sent to Beijing for review within a few days, and the public release period will also be in the near future.

The preliminary review of "Mother" has already passed. Although the re-review script has been printed, Mr. Shao Cunren and directors Wen Yimin, Gao Lihen, and Gao Tianqi discussed at the production meeting and believed that there were still inevitable shortcomings. In order to improve the script, it still needs to be revised. Therefore, Mr. Gao Tianqi has been responsible for the revision, reprinting, and submitting it for review.
